Northwest transportation urgently needs to be developed. That evening, Gu and Chen took the Longhai train west, heading to Tongguan and Huayin, respectively. (10th)

He Jian Requests Prior Reorganization and Dismissal of the Fourth Route Army

Chiang's Reply Telegram Does Not Approve

Changsha Communication: He Jian, commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army, originally commanded the 15th, 16th, and 19th divisions. After the second recovery of Changsha, he added the 31st and 32nd divisions, totaling five divisions. Commander-in-Chief Chiang recently appointed Wang Jinyu as the bandit suppression supervisor of the Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi border areas, and Xu Yuanquan as the bandit suppression supervisor of the Hunan, Hubei, and Sichuan border areas. The troops under the jurisdiction of the Fourth Route Army, such as Wang Dongyuan's 15th Division, have entered Tongxiu, Jiangxi from Pingjiang. Tao Guang's 31st Division has entered Tongcheng, Hubei from Pingjiang, and then turned to Xiushui, Jiangxi. Chen Guangzhong's 32nd Division has entered Wanzai, Jiangxi from Liuyang. In fact, they are all within the area under Wang Jinyu's command. Li Jue's 19th Division has been in Gongan and Songzi, Hubei from Liling. In fact, it is within the area under Xu Yuanquan's command. Therefore, He Jian believed that since bandit suppression work has established border area supervisors and divided areas for suppression, and all units of the Fourth Route Army to suppress the rebellion have also been assigned commanders, the title of commander-in-chief is unnecessary. He specially telegraphed Commander-in-Chief Chiang and Director He, requesting that an order be issued to abolish it, and that all troops be handed over to the two supervisors Wang and Xu to command bandit suppression. At the same time, he also sent Song Heceng, director of the Department of Construction, and Yu Kedong, a special representative of the headquarters stationed in Hunan, to Beijing to present everything to Chairman Chiang, but the reply telegram was received and was not approved. The text of the telegram is as follows: He Jian telegraphed: "Since the end of the campaign to suppress the rebels, Your Excellency has mobilized a large army to suppress the communists. Wherever your virtue has reached, good news has been frequently reported. Recently, the establishment of border area supervisors and the division of areas for suppression have been successful, and you are particularly admirable. The various troops of the subordinate Route Army will immediately transfer to the command of the two supervisors Wang and Xu and strive to complete their missions. I am relieved, but I have been ordered to command the affairs of the Fourth Route Army for two years, and I am ashamed to have not achieved an inch of merit. I am always fearful of being in a deep abyss. I have previously requested to resign, but have not been approved. Now, fortunately, the rebellion has been eliminated, and the remaining bandits can be annihilated. It is proposed that an order be issued to abolish the title of commander-in-chief of the Fourth Route Army to be a prelude to reorganization and dismissal. In addition to the current progress of the various troops and the various situations of undertaking tasks in accordance with the order, I have specially entrusted Councilor Yu Kedong, Correspondent Zhou Wei, and Councilor Hu Haichun to present them on my behalf, and I have also requested Director Song Heceng to go to the Garrison Headquarters to see Director He. I respectfully telegraph this for your review and order to be followed." Commander-in-Chief Chiang replied by telegram: "The three provinces of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are currently in the midst of bandit suppression. The reduction and reorganization should be carried out after the bandit suppression has come to an end. I have already telegraphed Director He of the Wuhan Garrison Headquarters to telegraph the various commander-in-chiefs, army commanders, and division commanders of the three provinces to comply with this order. Your request will not be discussed for the time being." He Chengjuan replied by telegram: "The reduction and reorganization of the army should be implemented, but Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi are currently in the midst of bandit suppression. I have received a telegram from the Commander-in-Chief stating that the reduction and reorganization will be carried out after the bandit suppression has come to an end. As for the division of areas, although it has been determined by order of the Headquarters, the various troops of the Fourth Route Army are still under your command due to the actual situation. I have arranged for Yu Wanxing (Wang Jinyu), Ling Bing (Xia Douyin), Su (Liu Wendao), and Funan (Song Heceng) to come to Hunan by train. We will discuss the rest in person." (7th)

The Unified Tax Bureau of Shandong and Henan Established in Qingdao

Office Opens and Taxes Collected Starting on the 1st

Qingdao Communication: The Ministry of Finance has issued a general order to all provinces and cities across the country that likin will be abolished starting on January 1st of this year. The various tax bureaus in Qingdao City have complied with the order and closed. The Ministry of Finance has sent personnel to establish the Unified Tax Bureau of Shandong and Henan, and has appointed Shen Yaorong as the director and Lu Xiaomie as the deputy director. Pan and Lu arrived in Qingdao a few days ago. The bureau is temporarily located at 37 Yangxin Road and began operations on January 1st, collecting various taxes. It is reported that the unified tax will include five items: cigarettes, wheat flour, cotton yarn, matches, and cement. Currently, only taxes on cigarettes and wheat flour are being collected. As for cotton yarn, matches, and cement, the Ministry of Finance has not yet issued collection methods, so it is not convenient to implement them at this time. The bureau has handled various matters properly and will begin to implement uniform taxation once the order from the Ministry arrives in Qingdao. (January 7th)

Clearing of Communist Bandits in Huoqiu Completed

Bengbu Dispatch: The Communist bandits of Hubei and Henan provinces once invaded Liu'an from Jinzhai last month but were jointly repelled by the defense army and local militia. They fled north through Mabao and gathered thousands more, attempting to seize Huoqiu. They first captured Baitafan, then successively occupied towns such as Kaishun Street and Yejiaji. The county seat of Huoqiu was in imminent danger. Ni Qihua, the magistrate of Huoqiu County, and various organizations and groups, seeing the momentum of the Communist bandits approaching the city walls, and the thin forces of the city's militia, which were difficult to resist, repeatedly telegraphed Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Anhui Northern Garrison in Bengbu, requesting that he quickly send capable troops to the rescue. Wei immediately dispatched Song Shike, commander of the Third Detachment, leading the First Regiment under Cheng Yi and the Second Regiment under Wang Shaoji, to proceed along the Zhengyang-Huoqiu line at the beginning of this month to suppress the bandits. Cheng's regiment advanced towards Yejiaji and engaged a small portion of the Communist bandits at Sunjiagang. They surrounded and suppressed them, killing more than ten on the spot and seizing twelve fast rifles and seventeen miscellaneous rifles. The Communist bandits in Baitafan were also routed by two battalions of Cheng's regiment, Wang and Hu. The bandits in Yejiaji fled back to Jinzhai upon hearing the news. Cheng's regiment continued to pursue and suppress them, while Song Shike led a portion of Wang's regiment to garrison at Lulimiao for defense and suppression. Now, the Communist bandits in Huoqiu have been completely cleared. (January 10)

New Japanese Plan for Managing Yanbian

Immigrating to Northern Korea

Expediting the Xiongxun Railway

Jilin Communication: According to a report from the Consulate in Seoul, Korea, to the Provincial Government of Heilongjiang, the Japanese Immigrant Company has been making unremitting efforts to promote immigration to Korea. Companies such as the Oriental Development Company and the Overseas Immigration Association plan to relocate a large number of Japanese people from the mainland to the Hamgyong North and South provinces of Korea, starting from the year 20 of the Republic (1931). According to their plan, the Tokyo Overseas Association will relocate 28 families to Shinan Township, Hamgyong North Province, next year, granting each family eight cho of reclaimed land (one cho is approximately 16 mu in China). The Oriental Development Company will transfer 65 families from Japan to Hamgyong North and South provinces next year, granting a total of more than 600 cho of reclaimed land. The Governor-General of Korea plans to establish an agricultural experiment station in Kapsan County, Hamgyong South Province, with a budget of 200,000 yuan next year, to reclaim fields around Mount Paektu and improve Korean agriculture. This is currently being planned by the Colonial Affairs Bureau. These immigration companies are nominally commercial organizations, but in essence, they are semi-official. The Japanese authorities' policy is simply to relocate Japanese people to Korea and drive Korean people to the Yanji area of China, acting as pioneers in implementing their policies. According to recent surveys, many Korean settlers in Yanji mortgage their real estate to the Japanese Oriental Development Company for loans, and about eight out of ten are unable to repay and have their property confiscated by the Japanese. Due to the lack of knowledge of the Korean people in Korea and the increasing number of Japanese coming to Korea in recent years, Koreans are often forced by livelihood to mortgage their land to the company as the only channel for financial accommodation. However, they do not know that if they fail to repay by the due date, the company will immediately confiscate their land and mortgage under the pretext of reorganization. Therefore, most of the Korean people who have fled to the Yanbian area of China have been oppressed by this immigration company. For example, the Korean riots that occurred in Tanchon County, Hamgyong South Province, last month, in which dozens of Korean farmers besieged a Japanese police station, were triggered by the immigration company forcibly confiscating their land and ordering them to leave, which aroused resentment among the Korean farmers. These so-called famine refugees, who have no foothold in Korea, come to the Yanbian area of China, where their livelihood is unstable. Moreover, due to various factors such as their status, their thoughts are abnormally excited. They are easily incited by others, blindly following and acting impulsively, and have been exploited. This year, there have been repeated cases of Korean communist bandits and riots. The root cause is that the number of Korean people who have fled to the Yanbian area of China is increasing year by year. In addition, the eastern section of the Tumen River Railway, from Unggi to Hunchun, was completely completed on December 1. Japanese officials and businessmen held a railway opening ceremony in Hunchun on that day. The Japanese began to build this line in the 17th year of the Republic (1928) and have only now completed it. Regarding the Jihui Railway issue, the Japanese, seeing the intense nationalist sentiment in China, are temporarily maintaining a wait-and-see attitude on the surface, but they have not abandoned their intention to achieve their goal. They are racking their brains to implement their plan. This Hunchun to Unggi line is also the base line for the future Jihui Railway. The Tumen River Railway can be divided into two parts: the eastern line and the western line. The eastern line, from Hoeryong to Sangsambong, is planned to be converted to a broad gauge so that it can directly reach Sangsambong from Chongjin, avoiding the hassle of changing trains. The western line, from Hunchun to Tonggwanzhen, is planned to begin construction next January. The Provincial Government believes that the influx of Korean墾 refugees into China not only increases the hidden dangers on the border but also develops transportation on the west coast of North Korea and connects with the atmosphere of Hunchun, which is of great importance to national defense and sovereignty. Therefore, it has issued a notice to all counties in Yanbian to investigate and take precautions as appropriate.

Zhejiang Province Prepares to Implement Business Tax

Scheduled to Convene a Business Tax Discussion Meeting

Zhejiang Province was the earliest to prepare for the abolition of likin, starting preparations in early 18th year of the Republic (1929), advocating the creation of a business tax to make up for the loss. The former Finance Department of Zhejiang Province established a Preparatory Committee for the Abolition of Likin to discuss and proceed. A method was agreed upon to start with commercial registration. The registration matters were entrusted to local chambers of commerce to handle on behalf. Later, due to the business community's concerns, no agreement was reached, and the matter was suspended. Now that likin has been abolished, the Provincial Government is determined to implement a business tax to supplement local revenue. However, since this is a new undertaking, the steps for implementation must be discussed in detail. Therefore, it has been decided to hold a meeting at the Finance Department on the 19th of this month to discuss the matter. The Provincial Government has already sent letters to leaders of various industries and economic experts, soliciting opinions on the creation of a business tax, to gather opinions from all parties and set a standard for implementation. The circular stated roughly: "Zhejiang Province is planning to create a business tax, and although a rough framework has been established, since this is a new undertaking, detailed discussion is necessary. The interests of businesses and the social economy should also be taken into account, so that implementation will be convenient in the future. Therefore, it is specifically scheduled to hold a business tax discussion meeting at the Finance Department at 2:00 PM on the 19th of this month. You are cordially invited to attend and provide guidance." It is said that the invited personnel include Ma Yinchu from Nanjing, Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jiji, and Xu Shusen from Shanghai, Wang Zhuzhai, Wang Xiangquan, Jin Shunquan, Zhu Mouxian, Han Zhirong, and Xu Qingfu from Hangzhou, as well as the chairmen of the chambers of commerce of Jiaxing, Huzhou, Shaoxing, Ningbo, and other places, totaling 34 people. The Finance Department will be represented by Wang Jiying, Wei Songtang, Xu Maolai, and Shen Ruji, totaling four people. It is also heard that the Provincial Government plans to implement the business tax jointly with officials and businesses, with a quota of 10 million yuan, and has already held preliminary consultations with Wang Xiaolai, Wang Zuyao, Jin Runquan, and Shen Weizhen.

Songjiang

A Police Officer Steals a Gun and Falsely Accuses Residents of Zhapunan Hougang

Mao Yongchang (from Zhejiang), a police officer of the County Police 第wv Squad stationed in Zhapu, stole a wooden-cased gun from the deputy squad leader and hid it elsewhere, intending to transport it elsewhere. The squad leader brought all the witnesses to the county government for interrogation, and the truth came to light. The initial step is to investigate the capital and total business volume of merchants as a basis for taxation. Miro Pavilion to be Renovated as Zhongshan Hall, Designs Solicited

The site of the original Miro Pavilion of the Yuemiao Temple in Suzhou is being renovated into Zhongshan Hall through fundraising. The architectural design and scope have been determined. The style and appearance must be grand and magnificent, preserving the inherent characteristics of Chinese architecture while innovating. The design must not lose its commemorative meaning and must accommodate 1,500 people, with a stage in the center, two side rooms, and one entertainment room, and two women's restrooms. The County Government has set a deadline of January 10 for the submission of designs, which will be extended to January 15, to facilitate fundraising and begin construction.

Amnesty for Political Prisoners

The Higher Court Review Committee received an order from the Ministry of Justice on the 6th of this month, ordering that within seven days of receipt of the document, all political prisoners detained in prisons in various counties who meet the amnesty regulations should be organized to form a review committee to verify the facts, provide bail, and release them. After receiving the order, President Lin of the court immediately formed a review committee with Chief Prosecutor Wang Simo, Prosecutor Jin Henian, and Criminal Court President Lin Dawen. He also issued a notice to the wardens of various county prisons yesterday (the 12th), requiring them to report the list of political prisoners in custody within three days of receipt of the document to facilitate verification and release.

Higher Court Petitions the Ministry for Relief of Prisons

President Lin of the Higher Court stated that according to statistics, the prisons in Jiangsu Province are newly built and that the number of prisoners detained has reached more than 24,000, which is more than double the number in 1928. All prisons are overcrowded, making it difficult to add more prisoners. If relief measures are not taken, the lives of the prisoners in custody are in extreme danger. Therefore, yesterday (the 12th), he specifically petitioned the Ministry of Justice, requesting that relief measures be taken immediately.

Wuxi

Resignation of All Township Chiefs in the County

The township chiefs of Wuxi, including Qian Zongliang, recently submitted a joint resignation to the county government due to financial exhaustion and difficulty in handling affairs. The petition stated roughly that the matters ordered to be handled by the townships were increasing day by day, while the administrative and operational expenses of the townships were decreasing. The purpose of the township chiefs going to the province to receive training was to handle local affairs. Now that the funding situation is like this, the results are contrary to their wishes. Even if they want to work hard for the public, it is like trying to cook without rice. Exhausted both mentally and physically, it is difficult to maintain. In desperation, they have no choice but to jointly submit their resignations, requesting the appointment of other capable people to take over. It is not known what Director Pan of the County will decide.

Philanthropists Provide Relief to the Poor

Since the 10th of this month, Wuxi has been experiencing heavy snow and extremely cold weather. Some of the poor and prisoners in prison have already died from the cold. Ji Yunqing, a native of Wuxi in Shanghai, has initiated a winter relief effort, raising donations of clothing and rice in both Wuxi and Shanghai. He also plans to hold a three-day theatrical performance, with all the proceeds going to the relief effort. He has already advanced funds to purchase rice and will start distributing porridge immediately. He has also asked Du Yuesheng, a well-known figure in Shanghai, to donate a large number of cotton-padded clothes and quilts to be distributed to the prisoners in prison in Wuxi to help them keep warm. The Red Swastika Society has also advanced the distribution of rice tickets to help the poor.

Meat Industry Requests Suspension of Slaughter Tax

The Wuxi Meat Industry Association recently stated that since the government is implementing the abolition of likin and the introduction of a business tax, according to Article 7 of the Guidelines for the Preparation of a Business Tax by the Likin Abolition Committee of the Ministry of Finance, after the business tax is implemented, all existing license taxes, stamp taxes, slaughter taxes, and other taxes similar to the business tax in various provinces should be merged or abolished separately. The association is currently petitioning to change to a business tax. All previously donated slaughter taxes, construction special donations, and local taxes should be abolished, just like the abolished tax authorities. They have specially requested the county chamber of commerce to forward the petition to the Finance Department, requesting that all previously donated taxes be abolished from January 1st to comply with the central government's policy of one tax per item and to abolish excessive taxes and miscellaneous levies, thereby alleviating the burdens on businesses and maintaining business operations.

Changzhou

Citywide Restaurant Strike

The restaurant industry in Wuyi County is dissatisfied with the collection of banquet taxes by the Banquet Tax Collection Office. On the evening of the 11th, the Collection Office sent Deng Kaishi, an employee of the Luyang Restaurant on Renyu Bridge, to the First Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which caused the city's industry to immediately hold a meeting at the Restaurant Association to discuss countermeasures. It was decided that all businesses in the city would go on strike starting on the 12th. However, businesses that provide catering services will suspend operations from the 13th due to pre-existing commitments.

Burglary in Yaojia Alley

Wang Yongsheng's house in Yantang Village, near Yaojia Alley in Wuyi County, was suddenly visited by three bandits on the night of the previous day (the 10th). Each held a pistol and flashlight and broke into the house. They tied up Yongsheng and burned him with fire, demanding to know where he had hidden his money. Yongsheng could not endure it and handed over all the money he had prepared for buying property. The bandits then fired a shot to demonstrate their power and left.

Zhenjiang

Inland River Freezes, Small Ferries Temporarily Suspended

Due to the severe cold weather in the past two days, the inland river has frozen, and all the small ferry companies in this port have temporarily suspended their services.

Abduction of a Young Girl Cracked

Fan Shenshi, Fan Lanting, Bai Guangxin, Xu Liuzi, and Chen Fengshi abducted a young girl named Tang Guixiang from Xinghua to Zhenjiang, intending to take her to Beijing for sale. They stayed at the Jinlong Inn in Zhonglengquan Alley last night and were discovered by Xu Chunrong, a patrol officer of the Third Section of the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau. After interrogation, they confessed to being greedy and having an unclear background. The young girl Tang Guixiang confessed to being abducted. Xu believed that the case was related to abduction and sent Fan Shenshi and the other four people, along with the young girl Tang Guixiang, to the branch for handling.

Yangzhou

Petition Delegation Goes to Beijing to Fight for the Transportation Department

The various circles of Yangzhou believe that the Huai Transportation Department will move to northern Jiangsu. In addition to separately telegraphing the National Government and the Ministry of Finance to fight for it, they held a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce on the morning of the 11th to elect representatives to form a petition delegation to go to Beijing to petition. Wang Jingting, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Guo Lanshi, Standing Committee Member, Pan Songping, Xia Xiaocen, representative of various trade associations, Ling Gengbo, Zhang Yunhe, Director of the Relief Institute, Yang Puqing, Wang Zhenqing of the Education Association, and Ding Shengwu, representative of the masses, were elected and scheduled to depart from Yangzhou on the morning of the 12th.

Extraordinary Cold Weather After Heavy Snow

After the heavy snow on the 9th, the weather turned extremely cold. The Fahrenheit scale dropped to 10 degrees on the 10th and rose slightly to 3 degrees on the 11th. There was no citywide freezing, and the canal also froze, with small ferries suspended. Elderly people over 50 years old said that three days before the winter solstice 38 years ago, it was even worse than this. The Fahrenheit scale dropped to 8 degrees, and the next day it gradually warmed up, rising sharply to 17 degrees.

Nantong

Water and Land Police Squads Encircle and Suppress Sea Bandits

A large group of sea bandits was discovered at Jiansha and Yugang, at the intersection of Nantong and Haimen counties. The water and land police squads of the two counties converged to encircle and suppress them, killing nine bandits, seizing three Mauser pistols and two handguns, and rescuing two hostages: an old man surnamed Cui from Taicang and a young girl from Changshu. The weapons and hostages have been escorted to the city.

Ministry of Finance Explains Land Reclamation Registration Procedures

The Ministry of Finance has interpreted the registration procedures for the reclaimed land of various salt reclamation companies in Huainan. (1) Cultivated land that has been used as farmland, has been paid for, and has been assessed and taxed, and is not subject to the demolition tax, will be registered by the county. (2) Cultivated land that has been used as farmland, has been paid for, but is still subject to the demolition tax, will be temporarily registered with the salt administration. (3) Cultivated land that has not been paid for. (4) Reclaimed land that has not been cultivated but has been paid for, or has not yet been paid for. (5) Unreclaimed land used for salt production will all still be registered with the salt administration.

Jingjiang

The Self-Defense Corps Mistakenly Beats Good People

The Self-Defense Corps of the Eighth District mistakenly arrested Xu Chongwen, a good person, when arresting bandits in Zhengdongwei the day before yesterday and brought him to the regimental headquarters and beat him severely, causing Xu Chongwen to be covered in blood and injuries. After someone explained, he was released. Xu Chongwen was humiliated for no reason and reported his injuries to the county on the 7th. There is still no proper resolution.

Director of Finance Bureau Dismissed

He Liangyu, the Director of the Finance Bureau, was dismissed for unauthorized receipt of business tax seals, and Chen Shunen was appointed to fill the vacancy.

Hangzhou

Director Zhu Leads Troops to Suppress Bandits in Shengxian

The bandits in Xinchang and Shengxian counties, Zhejiang Province, are mostly former subordinates of Zhou Fengqi. They occupy dangerous mountains and often harass the area, leaving the people unable to sleep peacefully. The Provincial Government, after deliberation, decided to send Zhu Mingtao, the director of the Security Department, to personally lead troops to suppress them severely, with a deadline of one month to clear them out. After receiving the order, Zhu led his staff officers and adjutants to Shengxian across the river from Hangzhou. The troops he took to Xinchang and Shengxian included the four companies directly under the Third Regiment of the Security Force and the Eighth and Ninth Companies of the Second Regiment, one machine gun company, one mortar platoon, and one special service company. All the self-defense forces and police in the counties of Xinchang, Shengxian, and Fengtai were under the command of Director Zhu during the bandit suppression period.

Long-Distance Telephone Will Be Managed by the Ministry

Since Zhejiang implemented austerity policies, merging agencies and laying off personnel to save expenses, there have been rumors that the Construction Department will transfer the Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Bureau to the Ministry of Communications of Zhejiang Province to avoid both parties wasting public funds and to avoid disputes. As for the difficulties of the merger, the first is that the Provincial Long-Distance Telephone Office has spent more than one million yuan. It is uncertain whether the Ministry can have this huge sum of money, or whether it will be allocated in installments. It is currently under negotiation.

Hangzhou National Goods Joint Exhibition Extended to He

The Hangzhou National Goods Factory Federation has been approved by the Shanghai National Goods Federation to participate in the Jiaxing National Goods Exhibition. Shen Yanzhi, Jiang Senyu, Shen Guisun, Zhang Zhichan, Chen Guohua and other five people have been designated. The participating manufacturers were immediately notified to extend the exhibition period to the 18th of this month, and they still took the early train to He.

Pinghu

Zhapu Ferry Opens to Sanliqiao

The waterway from Zhapu to Pinghu is currently being blocked by the Water Conservancy Bureau building a dam near Sanliqiao as part of the Tonghe dredging project. The traffic is cut off, and the Pingzhapu ferry is anchored there. Due to the inconvenience of traveling to and from Zhapu, the people have asked the Highway Bureau through the Business and Statistics Association to add four bus routes from Sanliqiao to Zhapu City to connect with ferry passengers.

Gao Tianmin Escorted to He Court

Gao Tianmin, a local resident, previously filed a complaint with the province against Shen Shihua, the county magistrate. The province then ordered the county government to detain Gao Tianmin first, pending the designation of a court by the High Court to hear the case. It is now learned that the High Court has designated the Jiaxing Local Branch Court to hear the case, so Gao Tianmin was taken away by the court on the 9th.

Fengxian

Discovery of Stone Coffin and Phoebe Coffin During River Opening

In the Mojiagang area, about half a li behind the Shenjia Garden in Nanqiao Town, the original Baiqugang and other ports are being filled in due to the passage of the Nanmin Route. A new port is being opened to the east of the road to facilitate circulation, and the Construction Bureau has submitted a report to the province, hiring workers to fill and pick up from January 1 of this year. Yesterday, in the Shen family's farmland, at a depth of about ten feet, a stone coffin suddenly appeared. The lid was made of yellow sandstone slabs, and the construction was extremely solid. The area of each piece was two zhang long, one zhang five wide, and two chi thick. It took many workers to transport it, and the gray sandstone wall that was built around was blasted open before the tomb area was visible. There were a total of three tombs in front and behind. The first tomb had already decayed, leaving only dry bones of men and women, as well as several copper mirrors, candlesticks, and incense burners. The second tomb was filled with water, but the vermilion coffin was still intact as new, but only the outer coffin (commonly known as the coffin cover) was slightly moldy. It was immediately transported out and split open, and there was also black stagnant water inside the coffin. After draining it and checking, it was a female skeleton with a hair bun in the form of a snail shell and a ruyi inserted. (The ruyi was a flat wooden style without flowers.) Next to it were two wooden combs (made of bird bones, with fine and even teeth). In front of the feet was a bronze round mirror (the back of the mirror had patterns of wild beasts in the center circle, and there were bloodstains all over it), all of which were undamaged. In addition, there was a carefree bed at the bottom of the coffin, which was the right length and had the same style as a window lattice. A round hole was opened on it, which was just right for the head pillow, which is said to have been used for the original burial. The material of the coffin wood has been identified by experts as phoebe wood, which is why it has been able to last for so long without rotting. However, the age and surname cannot be determined because there are no mining records available. However, judging from the tomb method and the snail bun hairstyle, it is speculated that it must be a request from the Ming Dynasty. The Construction Bureau has made wooden boxes for the female bones and buried them in a public cemetery. There are still one coffin and three outer coffins, which will be opened when the weather is clear to find out the truth.

Shaoxing

Civil Affairs Department Notice: Illegally Collected Reporting Fees

The various villages and districts of Daoxu, Shaoxing, etc., were illegally collecting land reporting fees. After Zhang Xiqian, a villager from Xicun, Daoxu, telegraphed the provincial government to complain, the Civil Affairs Department dispatched personnel to Shaoxing to investigate the matter in detail in various villages and found it to be true. The Civil Affairs Department has now ordered the county government to instruct the village chiefs and deputies of the villages concerned to be warned, and to order them to return the collected fees for writing the reporting forms in full.

Implementation of Special Tax Reform on Foil Categories

The Shaoxing Special Tax Bureau for Foil Categories has been ordered to be abolished and replaced with a business tax. The director, Zhao Xianglin, remains in office. It has now been implemented, and the tax rate will temporarily remain the same as before. Regardless of the regular or supplementary tax, it will be taxed at 15% of the business turnover.

The Defense Corps Solves a Robbery Case

The family of Gao Guisheng, in front of the Qinglong Mountain in Xicang, Xiaoshan, was preparing a dowry for his sister's wedding when bandits broke into the house and robbed them, injuring the mother. The value of the items robbed was five or six hundred gold. He immediately reported to the local defense corps, which stepped up its investigation. Yesterday (the 5th), two suspected robbers, Gao Aben and Gao Ahao, were apprehended nearby. Six types of stolen goods, including cloth and clothing, were found. The victim identified them without error, and the robbers confessed to the crime. The stolen goods and the robbers were sent to the county government for legal action.

Telegraph Request to Stop Illegal Collection of Rice Donations

The Preparatory Office of the Dayi Township Office in the Fifth District of Xiaoshan County illegally collected four sheng of rice per mu from the tenant farmers in the township as a mu donation. The Fifth District Office secretly assisted in this, acting in collusion. Farmers such as Wang reported this to the Second District Executive Committee, and after investigation, it was found to be true. Telegraphs were sent to the county party headquarters and the county government, ordering them to strictly stop it and investigate the matter according to law.

Shangyu

Robbery of Four Families and Injury of a Pedestrian

The Linhai Youheng Grocery Store in Xiejiabao, Dongxiang, was robbed around 10 p.m. on the 6th by more than 20 bandits armed with wooden-cased guns. They broke through the back door and entered, first grabbing a shop apprentice and beating him severely. They took over 180 small silver dollars from the silver chest. They then broke into the bedroom of the shop owner, Wei Fusheng. Wei had gone to the countryside to collect debts three days ago and had not returned. Wei's wife, seeing the situation was not good, voluntarily opened the chest and gave the bandits 160 silver dollars. The bandits then broke into the neighboring Taihetang Pharmacy, followed by the Xushengtai Rice Store and a certain cigarette paper store to loot. The three stores had been warned in advance and were only able to have their account boxes destroyed and some loose silver dollars stolen. When the bandits left the Dayouheng store, they encountered a water worker on the way who shouted loudly. He was shot with a gun, and the bullet went through his right wrist, causing him to fall to the ground. Soon, the sound of gongs and drums rang loudly in the street, and the bandits fled towards Yuyao.

Important News

Beijing Plans to Add Forty Primary Schools

Nanjing, 12th – The Beijing Municipal Government, in accordance with the central government's resolution on the construction of the capital, will start with the construction of primary schools and plans to add forty primary schools. Land will be requisitioned first to build school buildings.

Jiangsu Provincial Supervisory Education Association Holds Meeting in Wuxi

The third joint executive committee of the Jiangsu Provincial Supervisory and Education Commission held its second meeting at 9 a.m. yesterday in this city. More than ten people attended, including Mei Jieping, Education Committee of Jiangning County; Zhao Shiru, Supervisor of Zhenjiang County, and Zhang Fumin, Education Committee; Tan Wuzhuang, Education Committee of Luhe County; Song Yongsheng, Joint Supervisor of Wuxi, and Zhang Erwei, Education Committee. The Re-establishment of the Hangzhou Jisheng Midwifery School

The Hangzhou Private Jisheng Midwifery School, originally named Jisheng Obstetrics School, was founded by Principal Wu Chenyi. Since its establishment in the 14th year of the Republic, it has been painstakingly managed by Ms. Wu for six years. Ms. Wu is enthusiastic about education and has strong perseverance. The school's directors, Wang Zhubao, Zhu Xingwu, Wang Bihua, Wang Huafen, Zhang Xingfu, Tan Xihong, Fan Xiaowen, Wu Huikui, Zhang Xinpei, Zhang Xuren, and Wu Jianfei, have worked hard to maintain it. Their efforts are commendable. The school's board of directors submitted a request to the Hangzhou Municipal Government in July last autumn to be registered with the Education Department, intending to go through the school registration procedures. Unfortunately, Principal Wu fell ill and passed away in August of that year. The board of directors, seeing that there was no one to continue the work, immediately reported to the government to suspend the school. All students enrolled in the school were given transfer certificates to take exams elsewhere to continue their studies. However, the students of the school faced various inconveniences in transferring to other schools, and they missed the fine example of former Principal Wu. During the winter vacation, they united with their classmates to start a movement to restore the school so that they could complete their studies. They publicly elected Ms. Zhang Yuye and Ms. Zheng Hengbai to come to Hangzhou to earnestly request the former Dean of Education, Ruan Qiyu, to take the position of principal, and invited Yu Xiongfei to serve as vice principal. Former Director of Obstetrics, Liang Fangnu, took the position of Dean of Education. They worked hard to raise funds to restore the alma mater. Currently, they have borrowed Ruan's residence at No. 41 Gang'er Lane, Hangzhou City, as the school site. They have already published a notice declaring the re-establishment of the school. In addition to the unanimous return of old students, they have also published a notice to recruit new students, and the number of applicants is very enthusiastic. Recently, the new and old directors of the school publicly elected Director Gu Tianxi to pay a visit to the Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, Fan Qi, to personally report on the school's previous operations and the progress of this re-establishment movement.

Spring Council Meeting of the Vocational Education Society

The Chinese Vocational Education Society held its Spring Council Meeting at 6 p.m. on the 11th. Mr. Jiang Wenyu said that Mr. Yin Enrun and Mr. Liu Zhanen have always strongly advocated for success. It can be said that both gentlemen expressed their opinions. Mr. Yin Enrun explained the necessity of higher supplementary education. Mr. Liu Zhanen reported on the Shanghai University's plan to establish a business night university (divided into university classes, specialized courses, and special courses) and the situation of other places running higher supplementary education. Mr. Yang Weiyu said that it could be run jointly by several institutions. Liu Zhanen said that he represents Shanghai University and is very willing to cooperate with the society. Cai Yuanpei said that it is not easy to equip agricultural and engineering departments and it costs more. Mr. Yin Enrun said that the departments should be simplified and the business department could be run first. Mr. Huang Renzhi explained the difference between night school (completing the university course in a longer period of time and obtaining a degree) and higher supplementary education (supplementing higher applied knowledge and skills in a shorter period of time), and advocated that the latter is easier to realize and costs less, and can be run first. The former may start with advocacy and promotion. Cai Yuanpei said that it is best to use the existing Shanghai University night university. If it develops in the future, the business school of this school may be merged. Jiang Wenyu said that in terms of the agricultural and other departments, the existing night school should be reorganized and expanded. In terms of the night university, a committee can be organized to prepare first. It was resolved that the final decision be passed. One item: What kind of specialized subjects should be added to the amateur supplementary night school? It was resolved that on the one hand, the opinions of young people seeking knowledge should be solicited, and on the other hand, the talent needed by the employment agency should be solicited, and then the subjects should be determined. One item: How to help young people who are unable to go to school? It was resolved to propose work-study self-help and ask the office to formulate specific measures. Mr. Liu Zhanen proposed an ad hoc item: How should vocational education research be carried out more actively? It was resolved to continue to convene the side business education committee to discuss the method. One item: Military vocational training. It was resolved to hand it over to the office to formulate its own method. Mr. Yang Weiyu proposed an ad hoc item: This year's expert meeting method. China Science Society

Library Opens Today

The Mingfu Library of the China Science Society at 533 Albert Road, this city, opened on New Year's Day. It is now scheduled to officially open today. The library currently has 30,000 Chinese and Western books and more than 200 kinds of magazines. It is a public library, and everyone can enter the library to read books during the specified time. The reading rules are recorded below.

China Science Society Mingfu Library Reading Rules (1) Except for holidays stipulated by the Ministry of Education and Mondays, the library is open from 2 p.m. to 6 p.m. every day. (2) Anyone who wishes to come to the library to read newspapers and books can enter after a member of the society signs. Non-members deposit two yuan to obtain a reading certificate and sign in to the library with the certificate each time. The deposit will be refunded when the reading certificate is returned. However, if the reading certificate is lost, it will not be reissued. (3) Except for small notebooks, all items carried must be deposited in the deposit place and returned with the voucher when leaving the library. (4) When reading in the library, do not read aloud, walk heavily, chat, smoke, spit on the ground, or engage in other behaviors that disturb others. (5) The books and newspapers read must not be soiled, torn, or scribbled on. (6) After reading the books and newspapers, or if you want to leave the room before finishing reading, you must return them to your place. (7) If you want to read books and newspapers in the library, you must fill out a borrowing form and collect them from the clerk. You must not enter the library without permission and return them to the administrator for inspection. (8) Non-members of the society are not allowed to borrow for reading.

Soochow University Holds Commemorative Week

Submits a Plan to the Ministry of Education to Resolve the Turmoil

The School Motto is Changed to "Investigate Knowledge, Sincerity, and Correctness"

Soochow University opened on January 11 this year. The 12th was Monday. The General Manager's Commemorative Week was held at 10 a.m. All faculty, staff, and students attended. President Zhang Shouyong presided over the meeting and reported six items of school affairs and solutions. The situation approved by the Ministry of Education by telegram was also reported, and the school motto was changed to "Investigate Knowledge, Sincerity, and Correctness." The key points of the speech were that the former General Manager publicly declared on January 12 of the eighth year of the Republic, supporting the Republic of China. Today's Commemorative Week happens to be this day, so the four words "Investigate Knowledge, Sincerity, and Correctness" are the basic ideals for supporting Soochow University. In the past, the former General Manager asked Yangming to unite knowledge and action, so he encouraged people to manage, and his sincerity was good. Our school encourages students with this, which is also what the former General Manager called painstaking. Now that we have obtained the unique treasure in the knowledge of the political philosophy of the former General Manager, the four words "Investigate Knowledge, Sincerity, and Correctness" in the university are to promote a person from the inside to the outside, starting from the inside of a person and pushing it to peace in the world. This kind of spiritual development theory and should be based on the scope of the former General Manager's revelation. Soochow University takes this as the school motto, and takes the words of Zeng Zi's preaching, which is more profound than the previous theory of Yangming's learning. Students who come here to study should think from the big source and the big principle. If they can do these four words, there will never be any emotional events again. The former General Manager said in his speech at the Whampoa Military Academy that everyone wants to make trouble, but it is nothing more than saying that the teacher's management is not good and infringes on the students' equality and freedom. The former General Manager does not allow students to be free at all, because students are equal to officials and soldiers. Since I am the head of a school, I am like the commander-in-chief of the army. Soochow University has more than a thousand students. If there is no discipline, how can they be commanded? Therefore, when it is necessary to expel students, I cry bitterly, but I can only implement it. Soochow University's classmates are all kind and preserve the pure and good academic style, which is especially important. The things of the past are like yesterday's death. The former General Manager told people to be loving, sincere, and genuine. My classmates should especially use this to make friends and deal with the world. As for the teacher's thinking, under the rule of the party, the principle should be not to violate the party's principles. As for the future, when the period of political tutelage advances to the period of constitutional government, there will naturally be a fundamental law. Scholars who discuss politics should base themselves on the political system under which they are in. As for comparative theories, they can be developed themselves, but if they conflict, it is not allowed. This is also my deep hope that teachers and students will unify their thinking and encourage each other. The telegram from Soochow University to the Ministry of Education and the reply from the Ministry of Education are recorded below. (1) The text sent to the Ministry of Education said: "The Ministry of Education of the Capital is hereby informed that the situation of the Soochow University's turmoil has been reported. The solutions are summarized and telegraphed: (1) The school motto is changed to 'Investigate Knowledge, Sincerity, and Correctness.' (2) The commemorative week used to be inconsistent with the ceremony, but now it is held every week in accordance with the regulations. (3) Vice President Liao has absolutely nothing to do with the old cases in the Southeast. Vice President Yang of the Graduate School can prove it. Now that Vice President Liao has repeatedly requested to resign, it has been submitted to the board of directors, and it is planned to ask him to specialize in middle school. (4) The teacher's thinking should be more rectified. (5) The academic style should be more strict. (6) Once a student has been expelled, he is not allowed to apply for reinstatement. The school will give a certificate of study based on the seriousness of the circumstances, so that he can transfer to another school. The opening date of the 11th is very near. Please give instructions by telegram, so that we can do our best." Zhang Shouyong, President of Soochow University, sealed. (2) The Ministry of Education replied by telegram: "President Zhang of Soochow University: I have received all the telegrams. The Central Secretariat has approved this case and handed it over for review, and the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau has reported it. The Ministry is reviewing it. According to the six solutions submitted by telegram, the proposed solutions are generally in line with the requirements and should be approved. However, Luo Jiji, a teacher of the school, has made absurd remarks and repeatedly publicly slandered our party. It is not appropriate to allow him to continue to hold office. The school should immediately replace him. In the future, the school principal should also supervise the faculty, staff, and students to study the party's principles and unify their thinking in order to cultivate a pure and long-lasting academic style. The whole school students must be strictly warned not to take any more irregular actions. This is of utmost importance. You should follow the instructions and report the compliance situation." Ministry of Education, Jia.

The Xikang Class Delegation Arrives in Shanghai Today

Visits Factories and Scenery in Wuxi for Several Days

Provincial Mass Education Academy Holds a Welcome Party

The students were all very happy. It was originally scheduled to leave Ximi and Shanghai on the 9th, but due to the heavy wind and snow, the work in Xixi could not be completed as scheduled, so it was changed to arrive in Shanghai today (12th).

Finally, the students of the delegation participated in the performance of the Kangzhuang Song and Dance. The singing was melodious and the steps were neat, which was very interesting. The audience was beaming and said they had never seen anything like it. It is also known that the country will stay in the junior high school department of Shanghai Middle School in Ximen after arriving in Shanghai, and will have to return to Beijing in about five or six days.

Expansion of the White Goose Painting Research Institute

The White Goose Painting Research Institute, a well-known cultural group, has become more and more consolidated since it was registered by the Municipal Education Bureau. Chen Qiucao and Fang Xuegu, the directors of the institute, are actively preparing for the improvement of various affairs of the institute, sparing no effort. Recently, because the original location faced north and the light was not good, and the research room was not well distributed, in order to expand the scope, a four-story building was rented on Changchun Road. In addition to adding painting rooms, it is planned to add many dormitories for research members. The library and reading rooms should be well-equipped, and the outdoor space is wide and beautiful with flowers and trees. The researchers can take a break after class, which is very convenient. It is currently being decorated and will be opened at the same time as the fifth practice exhibition being prepared by the institute.

Mr. Zhou Tingxu Returns from Europe

Mr. Zhou Tingxu, a native of Siming, Fujian, went to the Boston Museum of Fine Arts in the United States in the ninth year of the Republic of China to study painting. In the twelfth year of the Republic of China, he went to England, entered the Royal Academy, and graduated in the sixteenth year of the Republic of China. He remained in England to continue his studies. His works have been exhibited at national art exhibitions in London, New York, Paris, Sweden, Scotland, and Liverpool. He has held two solo exhibitions in London. Mr. Zhou is also a member of the Royal Society of British Artists. According to the society's limit of only one hundred and fifty members, he was the first foreigner to be elected into the society, and also the first foreigner to receive the society's gold medal award, so he enjoys a high reputation in that country. He recently returned to his hometown to visit relatives and arrived in Shanghai by sea. He plans to travel to Peiping (Beijing) before going to America and then Europe.

Sports

West Qing Basketball Group B First Final

Shanghai Zhong wins after a hard fight.

Result: 29 to 20, winning against Xia Guang

Second final: Friday evening at 8 p.m. The first final between the champions of Group B1 and B2 of the West Qing Basketball Association was held at 8 p.m. last night. Xia Guang took the lead and soared. They led 14 to 9 in the first half. In the second half, Shanghai Zhong fought hard and turned defeat into victory. As a result, Shanghai Zhong won 29 to 20. The second final between the two teams will be held at 8 p.m. this Friday. It is difficult to tell who will win the championship at this moment.

Galloping Steed Overcomes Strong Enemy

Amidst the silver flute sound, Qian Jingyong of Shanghai Zhong cut in from behind, his foot on the line. Although he scored, it was invalid. Fortunately, luck was still on his side, and he made two free throws, breaking the record first. Kang Yuefa of Xia Guang invaded from the side and scored, returning the score to 2-2. Qian Jiexing, the pillar of Xia Guang, commanded the three armies. When the opportunity came, Kang scored again. After several exchanges, Chen Guangqiu and Kang Yuefa, the galloping steeds of Xia Guang, broke through the gate and each scored a goal. Xia Guang immediately took the lead with 8 to 2. Shanghai Jiang rested and planned, hoping to recover. However, they were too eager to achieve success and wasted many opportunities. Unexpectedly, Ren Jiexing scored another point with a free throw, and the score gradually narrowed. Qian of Shanghai Jiang scored a point with a free throw, and their morale was slightly boosted. Wang Gongying boosted his energy and advanced bravely, winning a goal. The score between the two teams became 9 to 5 (Xia Guang leading). Shanghai Zhong defended the key points, as solid as a golden city. Xia Guang had no way to get in and could only shoot from a distance. Fortunately, Ren Jiexing scored one out of one free throw, creating an advantage of 12 to 5. Shanghai Zhong made many throws, but they were distracted and the ball was not accurate. After a long time, Feng Nianhua finally scored a goal. Xia Guang also stopped the troops and rested due to the unfavorable situation. Afterwards, the ball situation was equal, and Ren and Qian each scored a goal. In the first half, Xia Guang led with 14 to 9.

Heroes Create the Times

At the beginning of the second half, Shanghai Zhong bravely fought back, with terrifying shouts. Feng Nianhua shot from the side and scored first. Wang Gongying raised his hand and the ball went into the basket. Qian Jingyong lurked deep under the basket, and a ball came from afar, which he turned around and threw in. With three goals, Shanghai Zhong finally rose to the occasion and took the lead with 15 to 14. Xia Guang then reorganized its line and fought again. However, Qian Jingyong revisited the old place and found the basket again, making the difference 17 to 14. When Kang Yuefa of Xia Guang was hoarse, he ventured alone and shot a goal. The two teams were one point apart. Qian Jingyong added three goals in a row, and the atmosphere suddenly became strong. The old and young of Shanghai Zhong accompanied the cheers, starting from all sides, as a pre-celebration for the successful efforts of these young heroes. Xia Guang did not give up and continued to fight. Kang Yuefa fought alone, grabbing two balls and making two free throws, suddenly making the score 23 to 22. The air was tense and the situation was serious. Feng Nianhua lived up to his mission and scored three goals in a row. As a result, Shanghai Zhong finally won 29 to 22.

Local News

Chairman Chiang Retains Commander Xiong

Still to serve as Songhu Garrison Commander

Hu Zuyu Promoted to Commander of the Fifth Division

Since being injured in an airplane accident, Xiong Shihui, the Songhu Garrison Commander, has repeatedly telegraphed the Central Government, requesting to resign from his concurrent positions as Garrison Commander and Commander of the Fifth Division. During the New Year holiday, when Chairman Chiang came to Shanghai, Xiong earnestly resigned in person. After repeated persuasion by Chiang, he was retained on the grounds that the Songhu area was peaceful and there was no need to send someone to replace him. However, the position of Commander of the Fifth Division was promised to be assigned to someone else immediately. Yesterday, the Garrison Headquarters received an order from the General Headquarters, officially appointing Hu Zuyu, the Brigade Commander of the Fifth Division, as the Division Commander. As for the Garrison Commander, Xiong will continue to serve. It is heard that in the future, after Xiong recovers from his injury and is discharged from the hospital, he is scheduled to be promoted to Vice Minister of the Army Ministry.

Design Committee Established

Decision Made at Yesterday's County Government Meeting

Origin of the Local Cold Wave

Caused by an Anticyclone Originating in Siberia

Comparison of Temperature Records from the Observatory Over the Years

Truly an Unprecedented Cold Wave in 38 Years

According to the Xujiahui Observatory, the severity of the cold in the past few days has been rare in decades. According to the observatory's temperature records over the years, only the lowest temperature on January 19, 1893, dropped to 10 degrees Fahrenheit, which is 1.1 degrees lower than last Friday's 11.1 degrees. In addition, although there were also extremely cold months in 1878, 1916, and 1917, they still did not reach the cold of this time. On January 4 of this year, the lowest temperature was still 53.1 degrees and the highest was 63.5 degrees. Afterwards, the temperature gradually decreased. On January 8, the lowest was 40.1 degrees and the highest was 42.8 degrees. The next day, the weather suddenly changed, with wind and clouds interacting. At 5 a.m., it was still 36 degrees, but at 9 p.m., it dropped to 26.8 degrees. On January 10, the highest was only 19.9 degrees and the lowest was 11.1 degrees. The difference between the two days was nearly 30 degrees. On the 11th and 12th, the weather was slightly milder, but the temperature remained below freezing. Even yesterday's highest temperature was only 30.4 degrees. The formation of this cold wave was due to an anticyclone in Siberia. Irkutsk, located near Lake Baikal, has always been the place with the highest air pressure in the world. This time, it reached 806 millimeters (normal air pressure is about 760 millimeters, which is the pressure of a 760-millimeter mercury column in a vacuum tube). As a result, the cold air moved south and spread over northern and central China, causing a rare blizzard. The seasonal winds that should have been present in the coastal areas during the winter retreated three times, leaving the area south of the Yangtze River estuary, becoming an unprecedented cold wave in 38 years. The cold wave in 1893 was also caused by the same anticyclone. At that time, the air pressure in Irkutsk was even higher than this year by one millimeter, so the temperature in Shanghai was also one degree lower. The cold lasted for a week before it began to recover. This cold wave is expected to last for the same period.

Wind and Snow Hinder Shipping

Baihe River Completely Frozen | Qingdao Port Closed

Xin Chang Breaks Through | Shangjiang Suspends Navigation

Due to the extraordinarily cold weather in recent days, land and water transportation in Shanghai have been hindered, and the shipping industry has suffered even greater losses. In the Beiyang region, the rivers are frozen, and shipping is impossible, which is rare in the past ten years. The information we have is reported as follows:

Frozen Ships. On the 10th of this month, the first day of severe cold in Shanghai, inland river and ocean-going ships were affected, and the impact on Beiyang liners was even greater. Yesterday, various shipping companies in Shanghai received a telegram from Tianjin, which stated that the waterways within Tanggu Port had been completely frozen overnight due to the storm and heavy snow on the night of the 10th. The ice thickness was more than ten feet. The lowest temperature was 14 degrees below zero. A total of twenty-one merchant ships anchored within the Baihe River, preparing to sail to Shanghai and other places on the 11th and 12th, were all blocked by the ice and unable to move. Not only were the engines of the ships ineffective, but even the icebreakers prepared by British and Japanese shipping companies could not break the solid ice. The ships were in a dilemma. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Feng ship was fortunate to have sailed out the day before and was not blocked. From yesterday onwards, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Beiyang ships have stopped sailing to Tianjin. That is, Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin, and Dalian ships also only go to Tanggu Port.

Ice Breaks Qingdao. The inner harbor of Qingdao has never been frozen. This time, due to the severe cold, the port has also frozen. Since the morning of the 11th, the inner harbor of Qingdao suddenly formed solid ice seven or eight feet thick, and horses and carts could pass on the ice. This is the first time in more than ten years. Yesterday, various shipping companies received a telegram from Qingdao, instructing ships going to Qingdao to reduce cargo and ordering ships to anchor only on the sea outside the port. All passengers and cargo going to Qingdao from Shanghai were transferred to the sea by lighters and then transferred by land.

Broken Ship. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Chang ship, on its return voyage from Hong Kong and Guangzhou, encountered a storm on the 10th while traveling in the Min Sea. The ship had recently been repaired and was very strong. On that day, the ship encountered a hurricane on the sea outside Fuzhou Port. The waves were so huge that they had never been seen before. The ship was hit by huge waves and almost could not sail. Just as it was about to drop anchor to a safe place to avoid the wind, a huge wave suddenly came, as if with the force of ten thousand jun, and hit the bow of the ship violently. With a loud noise, a large hole was broken in the outer hull of the Xin Chang ship, and seawater rushed into the ship. The passengers on board were shocked. Fortunately, the damage was in the head, and the hull did not sink. The loss of the goods loaded in the cabin was still small. Later, the shipowner ordered the sailors to pump water while facing the waves. They have now arrived in Shanghai. The cargo will be unloaded first, and then the damage will be inspected and the ship will be put into dock for major repairs. Navigation Suspended. The water level of the Yangtze River should have decreased in winter. Since the 10th of this month, there has been wind and snow in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, and the cold has increased greatly. The water level in the Yichang and Shajin areas has suddenly dropped sharply. The lowest point is only about six feet. More than a dozen temporary cargo ships traveling on the upper reaches of the Yangtze River from Shanghai have been ordered by the respective shipping companies to suspend services and return to Shanghai to wait for the river water to rise again and the weather to warm up before resuming services.

Silk Cocoon Industry Proposes New Tax Standards

Huang Jin Chen and Others Telegraph the National Government

Huang Jin Chen and others, the chairman of the General Silk Cocoon Association of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, telegraphed the National Government yesterday, saying: "To the Nanjing National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance: The people have long yearned for the abolition of lijin [internal customs tax], and now it has been resolutely implemented. All industries and businesses are rejoicing. We have read the multiple circular telegrams from the Ministry, implementing the abolition of lijin and all taxes similar to lijin. After the abolition of lijin, new taxes will be implemented, striving to conform to economic principles, one item one tax, and not hindering the development of industry and commerce. Considering this grand event, it not only eliminates the malpractice of more than eighty years, but also creates an unprecedented grand track since the tax system of the Han and Tang dynasties, benefiting the people's livelihood without limit. We believe that silk is a major export commodity, suffering from domestic and foreign taxes for a long time. From now on, we can hope to reduce the burden and strive for the evolution of work, in order to seek the development of the silk industry. Regarding the revision of new taxes and the adoption of standards, we would like to present our humble opinions to the Ministry: (1) Silk and cocoons should be combined into one tax. Cocoons are the raw materials for raw silk, and silk and cocoons are essentially the same item. They should not be taxed separately. If a special tax on cocoons is levied after the abolition of lijin, then the export silk tax should be exempted. If the silk tax is still levied, then the entire cocoon tax should be refunded in full, in order to conform to the principle of one item one tax. (2) The cocoon tax standard should be adopted in moderation and should not be proportional to the current tax rate. Since the 20th year of the Republic of China, the evolution of the Jiangsu and Zhejiang cocoon donation has been the shortest at five yuan per dan and the longest at the current tax of twelve yuan. The reason for this is that the old warlords repeatedly increased it. Not only were local petty expenses, but even military expenses had to be exceptionally borne by silk cocoon merchants, with the original amount being increased by one-third and the additional amount accumulating to more than 50%. This does not conform to the principles of tax law. If a special tax on cocoons is levied after the abolition of lijin, the standard should be six yuan per dan for the cocoon donation levied during the time when the late Prime Minister served as the Provisional President in the first year of the Republic of China, which is the most moderate. All local harsh and miscellaneous additions should be abolished together. We have heard that various countries in the East and West generally exempt industrial and commercial raw materials from taxes within the country, and the tax rate on export goods is even lighter. Today, the export of raw silk to Europe faces fierce competition from Japanese silk, and prices have recently been reduced to suppress Chinese silk. The near stagnation of sales since last year is all due to crowding out. If a moderate regulation on cocoon tax can be made and the miscellaneous taxes can be deleted, and the export silk tax can be abolished, the burden will be low and the cost will be light, so that industrial and commercial enterprises will have the opportunity to strive, and the production of silk cocoons will have the hope of development. We sincerely request the Ministry to adopt our humble suggestions, review and implement them for the benefit of all. Huang Jinshen and others, the chairmen of the General Silk Cocoon Association of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, kowtow and steam."

Current Status of Tax Bureau Collection

Sending Staff to Be Stationed at Various Factories for Collection

Daily Revenue of Approximately 50,000 to 60,000 Yuan

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, since the Tax Bureau of the Ministry of Finance started collecting taxes on new vehicles according to the new regulations of the Ministry of Finance on January 1 of this year, the results have been very good. Yesterday, a reporter from the Hua Dong News Agency visited Section Chief Wang of the bureau and inquired about the current status of collection. According to Section Chief Wang, only the two unified taxes on cigarettes and flour are currently being collected. The collection method for these tax regulations is to have the Tax Bureau send a number of resident factory committee members to be stationed at various cigarette or flour factories to supervise the collection, which can eliminate the malpractices of tax evasion and leakage. All factories, regardless of size, have committee members stationed there to accurately investigate the amount of daily output and record it in books using an accounting method. The factories then submit the records to the Tax Bureau every ten days or every half month. This method is based on the previous unified tax on cigarettes and is quite convenient and effective. As for whether it will be changed in the future, it is not yet known. As for the three unified taxes on matches, cement, and cotton yarn, they are currently under review by the Legislative Yuan. Once passed, collection can also begin. He also said that when the unified tax was first being prepared, there were some merchants who did not understand the content and sent letters or inquiries requesting a reduction in taxes. Now there are no such letters. It should be known that the collection of the unified tax is only once. After one collection, it can be passed domestically without obstruction. This was probably because they did not understand the actual situation at the time. The reporter then asked whether the five types of unified taxes currently stipulated by the Tax Bureau, namely cigarettes, flour, matches, cement, and cotton yarn, would be increased in the future. Section Chief Wang said that he had not heard of this matter and it seemed that there was no news of increasing other types of unified taxes for the time being. The reporter then met with Section Chief Zhong Jiu of the Third Section of the bureau and inquired about the daily statistics of the unified tax collected since New Year's Day. According to Section Chief Zhong, this matter is difficult to statistically analyze because each factory submits the records in an accounting format. However, based on the current situation, the daily revenue is approximately 50,000 to 60,000 yuan in Shanghai alone.

Taxpayers' Association Refutes the "North-China Daily News" Editorial

The Municipal Council Can Hardly Shirk Responsibility for the Rampant Kidnappings

The Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association, due to the frequent kidnapping cases within the Settlement, sent a letter to the Municipal Council questioning its ability to maintain public order. The "North-China Daily News" published an editorial entitled "Forgetfulness" on December 29th of last year, attempting a defense. It stated, in essence, that although Shanghai's police expenditure reached 4.7 million taels this year, with a population of one million in the Settlement, the per capita cost was only 4.7 taels, which was not significant compared to London's per capita police expenditure of one pound. In 1927, Chinese officials and civilians, as well as certain groups, sent letters to the Police Department praising their handling of kidnapping cases, noting that the number of kidnapping cases was 27, only three more than this year. Yet, the Chinese praised them in 1927 but criticized them this year, hence the "forgetfulness." Furthermore, the editorial stated that, according to the Chief of Police's report, when kidnappers negotiated with victims, they relied on influential officials and civilians within the Settlement as shields to avoid arrest. The newspaper also believed that the Ratepayers' Association's letter to the Municipal Council was intended to undermine the ruling power of foreigners within the Settlement. It is now reported that the Chinese taxpayers believe the newspaper's editorial lacked sound reasoning and contained many inaccuracies. Therefore, on the 7th, they sent a letter to the newspaper to correct these errors. The original letter is as follows:

To the Editor,

We have read your editorial "Forgetfulness" published on December 29th of last year. We find the points you raised inappropriate. (1) Your editorial mentions that while London's police expenditure is high, the cost of living and expenses in London are vastly different from those in Shanghai. It is difficult for Chinese residents to consider the per capita police expenditure of 4.7 taels per year in the Settlement as insignificant. Furthermore, are there frequent kidnapping cases in London? Or is it only Shanghai that sees them occurring so often? (2) The ineffectiveness of the current Police Department in handling theft cases cannot be concealed by citing letters of praise from years ago. The Police Department's expenditure has been increasing annually for the past six years, while the crime statistics have fluctuated erratically. Please observe the following table:

Year 1925 1926 1927 1928 1929 1930

Police Expenditure 2,279,099 taels 2,537,464 taels 2,937,118 taels 3,220,476 taels 3,861,180 taels 5,448,960 taels

Police Expenditure Increase Rate 100% 12% 29% 141% 269% 139%

Number of Kidnapping Cases 20 cases 5 cases 27 cases 49 cases 38 cases 30 cases

Kidnapping Case Increase/Decrease Rate 100% 25% 135% 245% 190% 125%

Moreover, the above-mentioned police expenditure is only part of the cost borne by the shopkeepers and residents for the city's public security. Due to the repeated occurrence of criminal cases within the Settlement in recent years, important institutions have hired gatekeepers, and wealthy residents carry bodyguards. Although these security expenses are not included in the Municipal Council's budget, they should also be included when discussing public security expenses within the Settlement. (3) The editorial states that influential residents within the Settlement act as shields for kidnappers. If this is true, then the Police Department has failed in its duty by not prosecuting them. If this is not the case, then the Police Department should not fabricate incidents to evade responsibility. (4) The editorial also claims that letters from various Chinese groups are intended to undermine the ruling power of foreigners within the Settlement. This is illogical, as the Municipal Council has both Chinese and foreign directors and should not be regarded as a foreign ruling body. Taxpayers pay taxes to maintain the Municipal Council and should have the right to supervise its measures, criticize its dereliction of duty, and promptly urge it to maintain public order. The letters from various groups to the Municipal Council merely express the collective public opinion of the Chinese within the Settlement. The rampant kidnappings and the decline of prosperity within the Settlement affect all residents, regardless of nationality. Evasive arguments are of no help. In summary, the urgent task now is for the Municipal Council to adopt active measures to fundamentally eliminate the problem. The entire resident community will certainly assist in this endeavor.

Recent News on the Unified Cotton Yarn Tax

Regulations Still Awaiting Decision by the Legislative Yuan

Collection Personnel Have Been Assigned to Various Locations

There is Talk of Implementing a Three-Tier Tax Rate

The "Nichi Nichi Shimbun" reports that the nationwide unified cotton yarn tax case was not passed by the Legislative Yuan at the end of last year. The Ministry of Finance originally scheduled to bring it up for discussion again on the 6th of this month. The Shanghai Chinese Cotton Mill Association sent two representatives, Zhang Zemin and Qian Chengxu, to Nanjing to negotiate. However, the meeting could not be held that day due to the large number of absent legislators, and no results were obtained. Therefore, the traditional implementation date of the unified tax, either the 15th of this month or February 1st, is still only speculation. In general, the tax will be implemented as soon as the regulations are promulgated. Currently, the cotton yarn of the various factories in Shanghai can still be shipped as before, as the abolition of likin has already been implemented in the provinces along the Yangtze River. However, according to news from the Chinese Cotton Mill Association, the Ministry of Finance's unified tax collectors for the various factories in Gudi have all been assigned. The Henan Yufeng Yarn Factory has even stationed troops in the factory to enforce the tax. Regarding the cotton yarn unified tax rate, it was originally set that 23 counts and below would be considered coarse yarn, and above 23 counts would be considered fine yarn. It is now rumored that the Ministry of Finance intends to change to a three-tier tax system, namely, 17 counts and below as one tier, above 17 counts up to 23 counts as one tier, and above 23 counts as one tier. The tax amounts will be 2 yuan, 3 yuan, and 4 yuan, respectively.
