General Assembly of Trade Association Representatives

Resolved to Abolish the Trade Regulations Committee

The various trade associations in this city, in order to fight for the issue of trade regulations, specially organized the Trade Regulations Protection Committee. As previously reported, due to the case of common compliance with the trade regulations of various industries, it was approved by the Executive Yuan. Therefore, in the afternoon, the third general assembly of representatives was convened at the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce. Representatives from over a hundred organizations such as the Southern Goods Industry, Intestine Industry, New Medicine Industry, Knitting Industry, Department Store Industry, Pollen Industry, Brick and Ash Industry, and Rickshaw Industry, including Zheng Chengqing, Ye Jiaxing, and Sun Choucheng, attended. Chairman Zheng Chengqing presided over the meeting. Chairman Zheng Chengqing reported that, "Representatives, today we are holding the third general assembly of representatives of various industries to address the issue of trade regulations. This meeting was originally scheduled to be held earlier because the trade regulations that we have fought for were approved by the Executive Yuan on December 17th of last year, as reported in the newspapers. However, the committee believed that the news was brief and uncertain, so it was decided to wait for the official approval before convening the meeting. At the same time, the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce was requested to organize a trade regulations committee to handle all trade regulation matters after the conclusion of this meeting. The approval order from the Executive Yuan arrived at the end of the year, so the meeting was delayed until today. We deeply know that trade regulations have a long history in the history of Chinese commerce. This approval is merely an added layer of protection on the existing system and should not be considered a joyful event. However, in the past, although there was a trade regulation system, it was ineffective because various industries could not use it well. In the future, we should follow the instructions of the approval order and use it well so that we can obtain full benefits. Fortunately, the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce has now agreed to our request and organized a trade regulation review committee. In the future, the trade regulations of various industries will first be reviewed by the review committee and then submitted to the official authorities for approval. It is thought that after this procedure, there will be a better path. This is a point worth reporting. In this effort to fight for trade regulations, all trade associations have been very enthusiastic and united, so the result is relatively satisfactory. We should recognize this process: that in the future, no matter what happens, as long as it is needed in fact and permitted by law, we must unite together and help each other to achieve the desired goal and increase the protection of our trade associations. Therefore, I hope that the representatives will not think that the trade regulation issue has been resolved today, and that this very precious and valuable spirit of unity will be dissolved. We must continue to increase unity, so that the foundation of our trade associations can be strengthened and there will be hope for the development of industry and commerce." After the report was completed, the discussion began and it was resolved: (1) to immediately abolish the Trade Regulations Protection Committee and transfer it to the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce for reception; (2) to establish a trade association consultation office as a place for inquiries and communication, but not to deal with the outside world in its name. The meeting adjourned after the resolution.

The Shanghai Municipal Trade Association Trade Regulations Protection Committee sent a letter to the various trade associations yesterday, stating: "To the Editor, all trade regulations approved for record by the various trade associations, whether or not they have joined the association, should be observed. This case has been approved by the Executive Yuan. The committee was organized by representatives of various industries as an expedient measure. Now that the trade regulations have been approved, the mission seems to have been completed. Therefore, according to the resolution of the third general assembly of representatives, starting from January 9th, all procedures can be completely concluded. In addition to cutting and destroying the seals, transferring the files and books, and the remaining funds to the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce for safekeeping, a report will be compiled on the progress, the approval order of the Executive Yuan, and a summary of income and expenditure. A copy is enclosed for your reference.

Shanghai-Nagasaki Telegraph Line Disconnected

80-90 Nautical Miles from Wusong

Submarine Cable Cut Due to Large Waves

According to Japanese newspaper reports, the Shanghai Japanese Telegraph Bureau announced that the Shanghai-Nagasaki submarine cable suddenly went out of service at 8:45 p.m. on the 10th. After technicians investigated, it was found that there was no obstacle on the landline. The submarine cable, located 80-90 kilometers from Wusong, was cut due to continuous cold weather and large waves. An urgent telegram has been sent to the Japanese Ministry of Communications to send personnel to repair it.

Special Shipping News

The "Xinfeng" Case Submitted for Public Adjudication Last year, the "Xinfeng" of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company was damaged by the Japanese "Kageyama Maru" of Nippon Yusen, resulting in a loss of 40,000 yuan. The company ordered the Tianjin branch to negotiate with the Nippon Yusen Coastal Branch nearby to claim compensation. For several months, the Japanese side has taken a perfunctory attitude and has not recognized the compensation. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has now sent a final official letter to Nippon Yusen, demanding compensation, and stating that if no decision is made, the case will be submitted for public adjudication. The Tianjin Customs River Department will also be requested to act as a notary to prove the responsibility for the accident.

Jiujiang Water Freight Agreed Last winter, six companies increased the shallow water fees on the Yangtze River. Among them, the water freight at the port of Jiujiang, due to repeated increases, has become even higher than the freight rate in Hankou, which has aroused the opposition of all Jiangxi merchants. The Xunshang Chamber of Commerce and the Nanshan Transportation Bureau have repeatedly telegraphed the various shipping companies in Shanghai to cancel the shallow water fee. The six companies convened a public meeting on this matter yesterday, and it was decided to reduce the Jiujiang freight rate by 12% of the current rate, while the added 15% shallow water fee must still be maintained to maintain uniformity. The Jiangxi merchants will be telegraphed today for verification.

Nanyang Chinese Ships Increase Troops On the Nanhua route, where there are the most pirates, British Tai Koo and Jardine have added twelve armed guards to each ship since last winter to protect the escort, making the journey safer. The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has also fully resumed the Nanhua route and is planning to add two new ships to operate the Shantou-Xiamen-Guangdong line. In order to ensure the safety of navigation, it has also been decided to increase the number of armed guards on each ship to twelve, following the example of British ships. Box guns will be used to protect the ship, and it will be implemented on February 1.

Anti-Opium Society Sends Letter to the Opium Prohibition Committee

Requesting Complete Prohibition of Opium

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Society sent a letter to the Central Opium Prohibition Committee yesterday, stating: "To the Editor, it has recently been heard from various sources that your committee has changed its policy of completely prohibiting opium and is now preparing to implement a national opium monopoly, which is shocking. On January 1st, a declaration of opium prohibition was issued to express the people's views. Our society hopes that the rumors are not true. The English opium prohibition declaration of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stated that the government is currently preparing to manage the national opium trade, and that in the future, the import and export of raw opium will be managed by an internal organization. The intention is unknown. Premier Sun Yat-sen's will clearly stipulates that 'the opium business can never coexist with the National Government that the people have entrusted with power.' It also states that 'anyone who advocates that the law should permit the opium business is an enemy of public opinion, and any responsible government agency that lowers the flag and ceases to fight against opium for its own private convenience, whether temporarily or permanently, is an act of betraying the country.' Furthermore, complete opium prohibition is stipulated in the platform of the Kuomintang, and the prohibition policy is also required by the national public. The National Government promulgated the opium prohibition law on July 25th of the 18th year, demonstrating the government's determination to prohibit opium. Although the implementation in various places has not been strong in recent years, such as the opium special tax in Hunan and Hubei, the open trade in Guangdong and Guangxi, and the cultivation of opium in Sichuan, Fujian, Yunnan, and Guizhou, which have been criticized by the Chinese people, the policy of complete prohibition should not be shifted due to this. Just as the saying goes, 'Do not refuse to eat for fear of choking.' The official statement of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to the outside world clearly states that the government is currently preparing to manage the national opium trade, which means that the government will recognize opium as a business permitted by law. If so, it will not only violate the previous opium prohibition law but also violate the Kuomintang platform, violate international treaties, and violate Premier Sun Yat-sen's will. Our society, which is engaged in anti-opium activities, has always taken it as its responsibility to express the people's wishes. This method is deeply unacceptable. During the recent Fourth Plenary Session of the Central Committee, the party and government officials made a resolution to strictly enforce opium prohibition. The government is right to vigorously promote the opium prohibition law, so that there is hope for the elimination of opium, to comfort the people who are longing for governance internally and to correct international public opinion externally. If the policy of prohibition is abandoned and the monopoly is taken as a substitute, it will not only be unpopular with the people but also contrary to the trend of revolution. Moreover, since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing, the Ministry of Finance implemented the opium monopoly in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. After several times of public opposition, the government resolutely decided to cancel the monopoly and sacrificed 40 million yuan in tax revenue annually. It also established the Opium Prohibition Committee to preside over the national opium prohibition. For the past two years, due to internal wars, it has failed to achieve results that satisfy the people, but the Chinese people can still understand its difficulties. Now that the internal wars have been quelled, it is a good opportunity for complete opium prohibition, but to make a plan for monopoly is truly beyond reason and something that our society cannot believe. It is still remembered that when your committee held the first National Opium Prohibition Conference two years ago, representatives of all parties in the country and people's organizations gathered together and passed 44 resolutions on completely prohibiting opium. Party and government dignitaries attended the conference and gave speeches, all advocating complete prohibition. If the monopoly is now implemented, disregarding the public opinion of the government and the people, it will run counter to the purpose of establishing your committee. Since January, people from all walks of life who are concerned about opium prohibition have come to the society to report, wanting to clarify your committee's attitude towards the policy of complete prohibition. Based on the resolution of the Standing Committee, we will request your committee to clarify whether the above rumors are true, in order to dispel doubts, and we will be happy to answer this humble request. With this announcement, we respectfully wish you good planning and look forward to hearing from you. To the Opium Prohibition Committee.

Red Cross Receives Jiangxi Disaster Report Yesterday

Extreme Human Tragedy

The Red Cross Society of China received a letter from the Jiangxi Fellow Provincial Disaster Relief Association in Yangzhou yesterday, requesting aid, along with a disaster map. The letter stated that the property loss was approximately 386,949,900 yuan, the number of houses burned was approximately 87,224, the number of people massacred was 128,075, and the number of refugees was 1,615,100. The above numbers were collected by the Jiangxi Provincial Party Department based on survey reports from various county party departments from May to August of the 19th year. Only 61 counties have submitted survey forms. The significant losses after the capture of Ji'an and Jingdezhen cities are not included. Jiangxi Province has a total of 81 counties, with 34 counties completely affected by bandits, 20 counties half affected by bandits, and 19 counties with bandits not yet cleared. Only 8 counties, including Nanchang, have not been affected by bandits. The relief request stated, "The comrades who are writing this are in a state of confusion and are unconsciously incoherent. In the past two months, they have been calling for help and running around. Even the loss of their parents is not as deeply painful. The disaster situation can be described as an extreme human tragedy."

Lide Oil Factory Scheduled to Resume Operations Today

Workers Have Accepted Government Advice

Xin Sheng News reports that regarding the labor dispute at the Lide Oil Factory in Zhabei, the Social Affairs Bureau approved the factory's dismissal of seven workers who had initiated the labor unrest, ordered the factory to resume operations immediately, and also ordered the labor union to surrender its registration certificate and cease activities. However, the workers expressed dissatisfaction and petitioned Party and government agencies, requesting the Social Affairs Bureau to retract its decision. To prevent the labor unrest from escalating, the city Party headquarters sent representatives to provide guidance, but due to the workers' insistence, no results were achieved. Currently, the Social Affairs Bureau, due to the union's failure to surrender its seal and registration certificate and its refusal to resume work, has sent a letter to the Municipal Public Security Bureau to revoke the license and issued a joint public notice with the Municipal Party Headquarters' Civil Training Committee, ordering the workers to resume work and approving the factory to hire new workers if the workers still refuse to resume work. It is reported that after the joint public notice was posted, most of the workers reported to the factory yesterday, so the factory is scheduled to resume operations today.

Local News II

Huangpu River Bridge Imminent

Floating Bridge Design Still Under Consideration

Copper Bridge Design Now Planned

Submitted to Authorities for Approval

Construction to Commence Upon Approval

Regarding the plan to build a bridge over the Huangpu River, the originator of the plan said yesterday that the project is actively underway, and the funds have been raised. Construction can begin once approved by the Municipal Government and the Construction Committee. The location is temporarily not being disclosed to prevent speculators from buying up land, but it will be near Dongjiadu and the Bund. When submitting the application to the Municipal Government, a design was attached. The design was originally planned by Mu Shuzai and others several years ago and is for a floating bridge. However, when submitting it to the Municipal Government for approval, the initiators believed that although the construction and cost of the floating bridge were simpler and more economical, bridge construction is a public service and not comparable to profit-making. Therefore, for the sake of permanence, it is intended to disregard the floating bridge design and commission a certain country's engineer stationed in Shanghai to draw a steel bridge design. Although the cost and construction are larger and slower, it is worthwhile for the development of the Pudong area. The steel bridge design has also been submitted to the Municipal Government for adoption. It is said that the most important reason for abandoning the floating bridge design is that it cannot last long, and another major reason is that the floating bridge design is not suitable for the Huangpu River, which is experiencing urban prosperity. The floating bridge design is slightly similar to the floating piers on the Bund of Sanma Road. Although the tide can rise and fall freely, the high and low tides will inevitably cause a tendency to be biased. Furthermore, many vehicles will use the bridge in the future. When heavy vehicles pass over this floating pier-style bridge in the future, the height will inevitably be uncertain. For these reasons, we are willing to sacrifice the original proposal and seek a more stable and permanent steel bridge plan. After the Construction Committee and the Municipal Government approve it, a meeting must be convened by the initiators and prominent figures in Shanghai who have participated in the project before construction begins. It is said that Zhang Jingjiang, chairman of the Construction Committee, recently sent a letter to Mayor Zhang Qun to discuss the matter.

Regulations for Civil Mediation in the Special District Court

Litigants Should First Submit a Mediation Request

Without Having to Pay Any Fees

Since the beginning of this year, the Special District Local Court has mediated all civil cases first. Only if a peaceful resolution cannot be reached will a trial be held. This innovative method will not only reduce the number of lawsuits but also greatly benefit the litigants. This is truly a good policy that has never existed before. In the past, plaintiffs in civil lawsuits had to pay litigation fees based on the amount they sought, sometimes amounting to thousands of gold. Although there were provisions for requesting assistance to temporarily waive fees for plaintiffs without such financial resources, it was a troublesome process. Now, it is no longer necessary to directly submit a lawsuit. Instead, a request for mediation should be submitted in duplicate. If there are two defendants, two copies of the request should be submitted, and so on. The original copy of the mediation request costs five cents of silver, and the duplicate copy costs two cents of silver. The difference in price between this and the current price of civil lawsuit documents is significant. Furthermore, no litigation fee is required when submitting a mediation request. Only if mediation fails is it necessary to purchase lawsuit documents and pay litigation fees in accordance with the law. Therefore, if the case is resolved through mediation, the cost of the documents is not as high as in the past, and there is no need to pay litigation fees. This is a tangible benefit for the litigants themselves. In addition, cases resolved through mediation do not involve delays or the trouble of going to court, which is an intangible benefit. Moreover, the qualifications of the mediators are very strict. Lawyers cannot be appointed as mediators to avoid the abuse of soliciting and manipulating cases. The general public believes that this method is truly good, but the lawyers' business will inevitably suffer a major blow.

Vegetable Seller Beaten After Patrolmen Intervened for Failure to Donate Certificates

Selling Vegetables Without a Certificate

Escaped into a British Home

Two Patrolmen Chased to Investigate

Beaten Up in the Kitchen

Li Jinlin, Qin Zanting, Wu Maomao, Xu Shengtin, and others, servants of British resident G. Wu at No. 1 Taopeng Road, were accused of assaulting Chinese patrolmen No. 1086 and No. 2708 of the Yangshupu Police Station. The case was tried by Judge Feng of the Special District Local Court. According to Li Zhishan, a lawyer for the Public Works Department, the incident occurred when Zhang, the wife of the defendant Xu Shengtin, was selling vegetables in the Pingliang Road vegetable market at 10:30 AM on the previous morning without donating certificates. The two patrolmen questioned her, and Zhang, feeling guilty, fled into the residence of British resident G. Wu with her vegetable basket to hide. The two patrolmen chased after her, but the defendants forcibly dragged the two patrolmen into the kitchen and insulted them. Chinese patrolman No. 1086 was stabbed in the left shoulder with a knife, and his clothes were torn, but fortunately he was not injured. Chinese patrolman No. 2708 was severely injured and is still in the hospital. He requested that the case be adjourned. The weapons, an iron bar and a sharp knife, were presented as evidence. Then, Russian patrolman Mike Lao Fu reported the situation at the time, stating that he heard the alarm and rushed to the scene, where he saw Chinese patrolman No. 1086 standing at the back door of the British residence, his head bleeding. He said that Chinese patrolman No. 2708 was attacked inside the house. He entered the house and saw the Chinese patrolman lying in the kitchen. The two defendants, Li and Qin, were still attacking him. Then, Chinese patrolman No. 1086 testified that when Zhang was trying to avoid the certificate inspection, she fled into the British residence, and he and No. 2708 chased after her. However, the defendants forcibly interfered and shouted and attacked them. Xu Shengtin struck him on the head with an iron hammer, and Li Jinlin stabbed him in the left shoulder with a knife. No. 2708 was knocked down, his weapons were snatched away, and there were seven or eight assailants. He jumped out of the window and was then assisted by Chinese patrolman No. 1049. Chinese patrolman No. 1049 testified that he was also at the scene when he questioned Zhang. Because the two patrolmen were chasing in front and he rushed over, the two patrolmen were trapped inside the house. He then used the telephone to report to the police station, and detectives were dispatched to help, and the defendants were arrested. Li Jinlin testified that the two patrolmen chased Zhang into the house and beat Xu Shengtin. He was also beaten for trying to persuade them and denied stabbing the Chinese patrolman in the left shoulder with a knife. Qin Zanting testified that he was identified as an assailant for trying to mediate. Wu Maomao also denied committing the assault. Zhang Shengtin claimed that it was true that his wife was selling vegetables without donating certificates, but he had pleaded with the two patrolmen at the time, but not only was he not forgiven, but he was forcibly beaten by them. Judge Feng ordered the defendants to be remanded into custody because Chinese patrolman No. 2708 was still being treated in the hospital, and the hearing was adjourned.

The Uproar Over the "Dumb Love" Film

Step-Mother and Elder Brother Dissatisfied with the Plot

Sue the Film Company in Court

The "Dumb Love" case of Lin Jiren and Wu Airong became a sensation in Shanghai after its successful conclusion. Subsequently, the Xishen Film Company, opened by Ren Xifan on Qingyun Road in Zhabei, filmed the story with Lin and Wu as the protagonists, and the parties involved also appeared in various theaters to speak about their experiences, which had considerable appeal. However, the film included a scene with Wu's step-mother and Wu's brother, which caused her step-mother Wu Yangmin and her elder brother Wu Baolun to feel greatly ashamed. They requested the court to ban the public screening of the film, but this was not approved. Therefore, Wu Yangmin and Wu Baolun were very dissatisfied. They hired a lawyer to file a criminal complaint in the local court against Ren Xifan, as well as the director Chen Zhuomin and the photographer Zhang Fukang, for defamation, requesting prosecution and filing a private claim for damages. Judge Ma Shounan heard the case in the fifth court yesterday at 10:00 AM. Wu Baolun and Chen Zhuomin did not appear, and Ren Xifan and Zhang Fukang also appeared in court with a lawyer. First, Wu Yangmin testified that she is 43 years old, from Guangdong, and lives at No. 9 Yipin Lane, Qiujiang Road. Wu Baolun is my biological son, and he works at the telephone company. He did not come today. Wu Airong is the daughter of Wu Guo, my first wife. The reason I filed the lawsuit is because the Xifan Company filmed a scene in which I beat Wu Airong, but I did not do that. There is also a scene that falsely accuses my son Baolun of introducing Wu Airong to Lin and later getting involved in the lawsuit. Baolun also acted as a mediator. My mother and son have been completely defamed. Originally, my family did not want Lin Jiren and Wu Airong to be together, so Lin Jiren received a two-month prison sentence, which was suspended. Now, they are making money using our names, so I request that they be convicted, the film be canceled, and damages be paid. Ren Xifan testified that he is 51 years old, from Ninghai, Zhejiang, and lives at No. 203 Qingyun Road. The Wu Airong film was commissioned by the Shishi Film Company to be filmed on its behalf because the company was newly established and did not have a filming location. Liang Zhongfen introduced me to them. In addition to Lin Jiren and Wu Airong, most of the actors were hired temporarily. Regarding the part about her brother and mother, I first asked the Film Inspection Committee to check it, fearing it would involve defamation. Therefore, I did not write that it was her biological brother but rather her cousin Wu Baolin, and the step-mother was simply written as Wu Airong's step-mother. The script was written by Wu Airong herself. She said that her step-mother not only beat her but also told her to have an abortion. What we made was that after Wu Airong ran away, her biological mother beat her, and her step-mother also hit her with a chicken feather duster. Regarding the part about her brother mediating, it was written that her cousin was the "most powerful mediator" because her cousin persuaded Wu Guo to accept the matter after Wu ran away. However, Wu Airong was responsible for the filming, but it was entirely because the Cantonese people in the Shishi Film Company saw that the deaf-mute man was very poor and would not even have food to eat, so they founded a film company and commissioned us to film it. Whenever Wu Airong went to a public screening, the court would persuade him after he won the lawsuit, and I would give him 50 yuan, otherwise he would have nothing, but he could not maintain his livelihood without it, so his biological mother did not object. The film is still in my company. Originally, there were also people from other places who came to buy it, but because the lawsuit was not yet settled, it was not sold. But my company is acting as an intermediary for the Shishi Film Company, although I manage it, the ownership belongs to others. Zhang Fukang testified that he is 25 years old, from Lanxi, and he photographed in the Xifan company. I am the director. I shoot whatever they tell me to shoot. I am completely not responsible. At this point, Wu Yangmin immediately said that the defendant said that he had changed Wu Baolun to Wu Baolin, but the pronunciation is the same but the characters are different, and the step-mother is me, and I did not give my consent, so I asked her lawyer to make further demands, saying that according to Ren Xifan's testimony, the crime is clear, and I requested that he be detained. The judge then stated that the parties involved in this case have not yet appeared, and it needs to be retried. Based on the plaintiff's request, he ordered Ren Xifan to post bail to be released and to be available whenever he is summoned. The case will be heard again, and then the court adjourned.

Strange Fragrance Fills the Room at Midnight

Doors and Windows Wide Open in the Early Morning

The Whole Family Sleeps Soundly

But Nothing is Lost

Chen Xingnan, a farmer in Qianhuang Village, northwest of Wusong, is well-off. Around 12 o'clock last night, Chen's wife, children, and others were all asleep. Only Chen was checking the accounts under the lamp in the bedroom. Suddenly, a spark entered through a crack in the window. Instantly, a strange fragrance filled the room. Chen smelled the strange fragrance, but soon his mind gradually became confused, and he lost consciousness. It was not until around 6:00 AM that his neighbors saw the windows and doors of Chen's house wide open and went inside to investigate. They saw Chen lying on the table, and his wife and children were lying in bed. They went forward to call them, but they were all sleeping soundly. The group was suspicious and strange. After the neighbors shouted loudly for an hour, Chen's whole family gradually woke up. When the neighbors asked the reason, they all stared blankly and did not know how to answer. Later, Chen recalled the strange fragrance he smelled the night before and was very frightened. However, Chen checked the whole family and found that nothing was missing. There were also no other strange findings, which was very strange.

Another Case of Coal Gas Poisoning

Residents Must Pay Attention When Burning Coal

Mrs. Xu, in critical condition. Mrs. Xu, a woman from Ningbo, over sixty years old, living with her daughter-in-law and eight-year-old grandson in a small room at No. 1, Tianlu Lane, Shunzhen Road, Zhabei, yesterday afternoon around four o'clock, due to the continuous cold weather, placed a coal briquette stove for warmth. The small room was filled with smoke, causing a nauseating odor. Before long, Mrs. Xu and the other two were poisoned by coal gas and collapsed on the ground. Mrs. Xu's right hand was burned by the fire, and a corner of her clothing was also burned away. Later, the second landlord saw smoke billowing and suspected a fire, and immediately notified the second fire brigade, which arrived in a vehicle. They forced the door open, and the firefighters sent Mrs. Xu and the others to Baolong Clinic for treatment. After the doctor's rescue, her daughter-in-law and grandson had already woken up one after the other, but Mrs. Xu's life was in danger.

Chen Fucai's wife died tragically. Chen Fucai, a man from Ningbo, around forty years old, who works as a boatman, whose residence is at No. 841, Xiaoben Lane, Fair Road, Hongkou, yesterday his wife was sick in bed, and a doctor was invited to diagnose and treat her. In the afternoon, they were decocting medicine on a coal briquette stove, and both husband and wife were poisoned by coal gas and became unconscious. It wasn't until around five o'clock in the evening that the second landlord, surnamed Shao, went to knock on the door. After a long time without a response, he suspected something was wrong and pried the door open. He saw Chen collapsed next to the coal stove, barely breathing, while his wife's hands and feet were ice-cold, and she had already died. He immediately went outside to call the patrolling police to the scene. First, Chen was sent to Tongren Hospital for treatment in a vehicle. According to the doctor, Chen had been poisoned for too long and his life was in danger. His wife's body was transported to Guangren Cemetery in a hearse and transferred to the coroner's office this morning to await an autopsy.

Sand Junk Sinks in Storm

Fourteen Crew Members

Rescued by Yantai Fishing Boat

Cargo and Hull Lost

Losses Estimated at Over 20,000 Taels

The large sand junk "Xu Changshun", loaded 450 large baskets of peanut oil from Qingkou to be unloaded at Xieju and Qiantai companies in Shanghai, was sailing past Tongsha waters outside Wusongkou at about ten o'clock in the morning the day before yesterday when suddenly struck by a "Yangjiao Wind" (i.e., a whirlwind), causing the boat to lose control. It was then hit by a huge wave, and the rudder was knocked off, causing it to capsize and gradually sink. There were fourteen crew members on board, and in the midst of the emergency, fortunately, a Yantai fishing boat came by, and they all shouted for help. The crew of the fishing boat completely rescued the crew of the sand junk, who took another sailboat to Shanghai yesterday to report the situation. However, the hull had already sunk, and the cargo had drifted away and its whereabouts were unknown. The losses were estimated at over 20,000 taels.

PEN Club Held Regular Meeting Yesterday Afternoon

Hu Shih Plans to Write Autobiography

The PEN Club held a regular meeting at Xueyuan on Jing'an Temple Road yesterday afternoon. More than twenty members and guests attended, including Di Pingzi, Yang Zhezi, Yang Lianggong, Xie Liuyi, Shen Congwen, Sun Liangong, Fu Donghua, Lu Kanru, Zhang Ziping, Li Qingya, Sun Dayu, Yao Mingyuan, Zheng Zhenduo, Zhang Zhenyu, and ladies such as Yu Xiuyun and Wu Kangru. Chairman Cai Yuanpei presided. Dr. Hu Shih spoke about China's lack of biographical literature, which had previously consisted mostly of official books becoming history. Therefore, on his fortieth birthday, he planned to write an autobiography. Although his life in a transitional era could not serve as a model, it could at least arouse interest. Rather than using distant materials, it was better to look within oneself, he said. He also reported that the Beijing PEN Club was in progress and could be expected to be established soon. Sheng Cheng spoke, agreeing with Hu's proposal, saying that his already written "My Mother and I," "Ten Years of Work-Study Abroad," and the unwritten "East and West" were all about developing national character. He described his impressions of traveling to Egypt, Palestine, Syria, Turkey, Greece, Mesopotamia, and India, believing that China was the only country in the world with a family tree, with an unbroken system for over two thousand years, so that the East could regain its glory through the Renaissance. This Year's Postal Employees' Annual Bonus Determined

One Month of Service Gets One-Twelfth of Monthly Salary

The Shanghai Postal Workers' Union requested an increase in the annual bonus for its members, which was submitted for discussion and resolution. At a meeting held the day before yesterday, it was decided that, starting from the twentieth year, postal workers who have served for one month will receive an annual bonus of one-twelfth of their monthly salary. The rest will be calculated by analogy, but the annual bonus cannot exceed one month.

Notes on Ship Accidents Due to Cold Weather

Recently, the weather has been unusually cold, with water freezing into ice. In addition, the west wind is strong, causing most of the inland small port waterways to freeze, preventing boats from traveling. The barge "Ling Genbao" was hired by merchant Jiang Rongji the day before yesterday to carry goods from north to south and seafood, etc., to Wujiang for

Page 16

unloading. It was loaded on the eleventh and immediately set sail. In the afternoon, it sailed to the south end of Longhua, and it was getting dark. At that time, the tide was high, the wind was strong, and it was snowing. The crew of the "Ling" boat had difficulty rowing due to the cold, so they sailed into the Xinkai River port to stop and avoid the cold. In the evening, Ling and two of his crewmates went ashore to buy things, leaving only his crewmate A Bao and apprentice Xiao San on the boat. At eleven o'clock in the evening, Ling and the others returned to the boat and saw A Bao lying stiff on the bow of the boat, not responding to their calls. Ling felt his hand, which was already ice-cold and lifeless, and knew that he had frozen to death. Xiao San was still breathing, so they boiled water and fed him ginger soup to resuscitate him, and he awoke. However, he had already become ill from the cold and was sent to the hospital and was still there yesterday. Also, the Ningbo firewood and charcoal boat "Fang Maohe" was carrying goods from Hangzhou to Shanghai. Yesterday morning, as it sailed to South Huangpu, the crew was rowing when one of them slipped and fell into the river due to the ice on the deck. When his fellow crewmen saw this, they went to rescue him, and two more of them fell in. Fang and the others tried their best to salvage them, and managed to rescue two of them. Before long, one of the crew members died from the cold. One crew member had not been retrieved, and his body has not been found to this day. The Salvage Bureau has been notified to search for it. There was also a flour boat named "Jinbao", fully loaded with flour, which capsized at twelve o'clock on the evening of the eleventh due to the strong winds and waves. Fortunately, it was near the shore of Luhui, and although the boatmen fell into the water, they were not drowned, but the losses were considerable.

An Improper Relationship Between a Man and a Woman

Arrested and Taken to the Police Station

Sometimes the sock machine breaks down, and she must come to Shanghai and take it to Zhenli Machinery Factory at No. 1412, Wai Ma Lu, Nanshi, to repair it. This led to her acquaintance with Zhang Xiaomao, the owner of the factory. Zhang, 31 years old, is a local and unmarried. He considers A'da to have good character and is quite fond of her. A'da also considers Zhang to be a factory owner, and her heart is also moved. So, it wasn't long before an ambiguous relationship developed. Then, the passion between the two reached a boiling point. A'da felt that traveling back and forth was inconvenient, so in July of last year, she secretly sneaked out of her house and went to Zhang, where she lived with him. Because Ye suddenly lost her daughter, she was anxious and searched everywhere, but there was no news. It wasn't until the day before yesterday that a friend told her that her daughter was hiding in the Zhenli Machinery Factory, where she and Zhang were living together like a married couple. Ye was furious when she heard this and immediately rushed to Shanghai, went to the factory at the address, and found A'da and Zhang together. She immediately went forward and dragged both the man and woman, howling, to Gao Diankui, the watchman at the 30th post. After inquiring about the situation, he took them to the first sub-bureau of the first district. The sub-bureau chief took the case and, after a preliminary examination, ordered that a written report be prepared and sent to the Shanghai Local Court for investigation because the matter concerned the abduction of a daughter.

Shop Assistant Chops Shop Owner

Xu A'da Transferred to Court

Zhu Julong, a native of Wuxi, 25 years old, opened a blacksmith shop named Zhu Juxing at No. 45, Nanjing Street, South Shanghai. He hired Xu A'da as a shop assistant. However, Xu was of a violent nature. The day before yesterday, he wanted to borrow one yuan from the shop owner for emergency use, but Zhu refused because he had no money. Xu harbored a grudge because of this and suddenly acted unreasonably. He then colluded with Peng A'er and, without rhyme or reason, beat Zhu severely. Xu even held a sharp axe and猛砍(砍) at Zhu's head, causing his head to be split open. Zhu fell to the ground in extreme pain, barely breathing. Seeing that he had caused a major disaster, Xu immediately fled. The watchman Ma Longyun from the 17th post heard about it and rushed to the scene. He arrested Peng and first had the injured person taken to the hospital for treatment. He then took the captured凶器 back to the first sub-bureau of the first district. After a preliminary examination by the sub-bureau chief, he ordered that a written report be prepared and sent to the Shanghai Local Court for investigation because the matter concerned assault.

Huang Bingheng to Go to Europe for Observation

Huang Bingheng, Deputy Director of the Aviation Administration, met with Commander-in-Chief Chiang in Beijing the day before yesterday. Chiang said that at the time when national defense planning was beginning, the increase of aviation strength was something that could not be delayed. Recalling the lack of domestic talent, it was necessary to cultivate true talent. He ordered Huang to go to Europe and America for on-site observation to advance his studies. Huang has now returned to Shanghai, sorted out his luggage, and will set sail for overseas in a few days.

Fire in Straw Shed on Guangzhao Road

A straw shed owned by a Mr. Zhu, who deals in second-hand goods, at a certain number on Guangzhao Road at the end of Hengfeng Road, Zhabei, caught fire at around 9:45 last night due to carelessness with a wind stove. The thick smoke was as dark as ink, and the fire became uncontrollable, spreading to the neighboring straw sheds. A total of more than thirty rooms were burned down. The first, second, and third fire brigades of Zhabei drove to the scene to try their best to extinguish the fire, which was finally extinguished at around 12:00 midnight. The fire starter was arrested by the patrolling police and taken to the Fourth District Public Security Bureau for submission to the Judicial Section for investigation.

The Paris Cinema on Xiafei Road has been showing "King of Photography," starring the cold-faced comedian Pei Sikaden, since it opened, and although it has been over a week, the box office has not declined at all. The film is full of jokes and is very interesting. It is said that because the next film to be shown has already been scheduled and cannot be changed, today is the last day to show this film, and tomorrow (Wednesday) it will be replaced by the European superstar Manda Songa starring in the Russian-Austrian military mysterious tragic film "Sun and Moon Brilliance."

General Ledger Published

At a time when our standard of living is increasing day by day, it is essential to balance income and expenditure economically. Therefore, statistics and accounting are the only essential tasks. The Guanghua Printing Company on Dongxi Huade Road in this city, in view of this, specially invited experts to compile a kind of general ledger, which has already been published and entrusted to the Bank Weekly Agency for sales. The content is organized according to the principles of double-entry bookkeeping, distinguishing between ledgers and more than ten kinds of forms. The subjects are clearly divided and systematically organized. Each is accompanied by a concise and complete explanation. For those who are familiar with bookkeeping, this can achieve accurate recording and detailed calculation. Those who want to study and practice can also use it for practice, so it is very suitable for family or personal use. Moreover, it uses a loose-leaf style, and the ledgers and forms can be freely added or subtracted, which is very convenient. The book cover is made of leather and烫金, and the spring is delicate, strong, and beautiful, making it easy to carry. The price for the whole set is only two yuan, and individual ledgers are also sold, at only 15 cents per bag. It can be said to be cheap and of good quality, and everyone should have one.

Publication of "Wenhú Special Issue"

Wenhú, that is, riddles, is the most interesting item of文字游戏. Literati and scholars all like to ponder over it. Hai Shang Shushi Sheng, Cheng Zhanlu, Fan Yanqiao, Cao Shuheng, Wu Shuzhou, and other gentlemen are all masters of making tigers. In view of the recent decline, they are all writing in their spare time to promote it. It was reformed and published the other day, with exquisite printing. The content includes "History of Wenhú," "Spring Lantern Tales of Wumen," "Five Tang Poetry Riddles," "Wenhú Style," "Wenhú Submissions," "Appreciating Riddles," "Tiger "作品，等词语, etc., about 20,000 words, all the crystallization of famous and valuable works. Anyone who wants to request a copy should attach five cents postage to the Shanghai Wenhú Special Issue Office next door to this newspaper, and it will be sent.

Notes on Fires

Pingjili Road At around 2:00 last morning, a red wood workshop opened by Li Shunlai, a Jiangbei native, at No. 49, Lan Fang Lane, Pingjili Road, French Concession, suddenly caught fire. The smoke was thick and filled the air, bursting through the roof. The fire brigade drove to the scene, but because the weather was cold, it was difficult to put out. It was not extinguished until around 4:00 at dawn. It is estimated that six houses at Nos. 49, 50, and 51 were burned down, and the losses were considerable.

Zhejiang Road Yesterday (12th) at 1:00 a.m., a traffic shoe and hat store at No. 460 Zhejiang Road, Public Concession, was careless with fire. At that time, the north wind was raging, and the fire took advantage of the wind, bursting through the roof and spreading in all directions. The neighboring No. 461 Yuanyutiehao, No. 458, No. 459, Louqing Pavilion Paper Shop, and No. 457 Xinchangxiang Clothing Store were all affected. Westerners from the Central Fire Brigade rushed to the scene with belt vehicles to put out the fire. It took a while to extinguish it. It is estimated that five city houses were destroyed.

YWCA Adds Tutorial Classes

The YWCA, in order to improve the knowledge of working women and to facilitate women who wish to specialize in one or two subjects and who cannot attend school full-time, has decided to add tutorial classes in Chinese Language, Mandarin, English, Arithmetic, Chinese and Western Music, Physical Education, and Cooking starting from February 1. The time and place of each day and evening tutorial class will be determined based on the number of applicants. Classes can be held on Nanjing Road or Dixiwei Road. Tuition fees are negotiable for music classes. Cooking classes are free of charge. Other subjects charge six yuan per semester for one subject, ten yuan for two subjects, and fourteen yuan for three or more subjects. YWCA members pay five yuan for one subject, nine yuan for two subjects, and thirteen yuan for three or more subjects. Anyone wishing to attend tutorial classes must register at the YWCA on the fifth floor of the Baoandi Women's Bank, Nanjing Road, before February 1. Classes will be opened at any time if there are five or more people in the same subject.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

Hai Ke

Millionaire (Very ill and dying, struggling on his sickbed.) | I'm dying soon. You must take good care of the money I leave behind.

Son | Father, I will naturally take good care of it. I dare not waste the money you worked so hard to earn.

Millionaire | People owe me a lot of money. Several notes. I will say their names. You write them down one by one. (So he said the names of several people.)

Son | I heard that Father owes people money as well. There are also several notes. Please say their names as well so that I can return them.

Millionaire | You don't need to worry about the money I owe people. When they die, they will naturally tell their sons about the money they owe people, just like me.

New Maid (Speaking to her mistress) | Madam, I don't want to work here anymore.

Mistress | Why? You haven't been here for many days. Why do you want to leave so soon?

New Maid | It's just that Mr. C comes to visit Miss every night. It affects my reputation.

Mistress | That's strange. He is Miss's boyfriend. It has nothing to do with you.

New Maid | But I am still young, and my face is not bad. The neighbors on the left and right are probably going to think that Mr. C is visiting me. Wouldn't that affect my reputation?

Girl A | Miss Wang owes the tailor a lot of money. She wants her fiancé to pay it off together before she will marry him.

Girl B | Then has he paid it off for her?

Girl A | He doesn't have that much money, so he is persuading her to marry the tailor.

A New Discovery: The Nose Can Tell Time

Chen Shuping

Besides those who suffer from syphilis, everyone in the world is born with a nose. But we only know that it has a sense of smell and is responsible for breathing. Unexpectedly, it also has the function of telling time. After hearing this, everyone must say that I am exaggerating, thinking that since there are no numbers marked on the nose, nor long and short hands, how can it report the time? You must know that the nose's report is entirely based on distinguishing between blockage and unobstructedness. Only you can feel it yourself, not report it to others. After I discovered that the nose's blockage and unobstructedness were related to the time of day, I began to study it in detail. I then learned that each nostril reports one hour of the day, and it is different for men and women. For the twelve hours of the day, a man's left nostril reports the hour of the Rat (11 PM - 1 AM), and his right nostril reports the hour of the Ox (1 AM - 3 AM), and so on. Women, on the other hand, are the opposite. The hour of the Rat is on the right side. The method of distinguishing is that, for example, when it comes to the hour of the Rat, we feel that the left nostril is more unobstructed than the right nostril when breathing. Women, on the other hand, feel that the right nostril is more unobstructed. When testing at the intersection of two hours, the effect is even more significant. If everyone doesn't believe me, you can try it on the spot. However, I must declare in advance that when you have a cold and your nose is blocked, it's like a cuckoo clock stopping, and you definitely won't be able to test any effect. According to the opinion of my friend Dr. Qin Jishi, the nose's ability to tell time is a normal phenomenon. There is nothing mysterious or strange about it. It is only because the human body is a very complex machine, and the flow of qi and blood never stops day and night, resulting in the nostrils' breathing blockage and unobstructedness changing at any time. This view has a sufficient basis. I am now recording it in Free Talk, sharing it with my fellow writers because I can't bear to keep it a secret. However, when clock shop owners see it, they will probably suspect that I am stealing their business. A laugh.

Good Character Warning

·Zhang·Gu·Chu

High-quality premium white rice: Lacks Vitamin B, easily causes beriberi and dampness.

High-quality tea leaves: Contains toxic substances, easily causes liver and kidney diseases, and makes it difficult to sleep.

Worry-relieving fine wine: Rich in stimulants, easily damages the brain and lungs.

Beautiful concubines: Nothing but objects that invite blame, the root of disgrace.

Comfortable automobiles: Turn and make blood flow unbalanced, sinews and bones inflexible. Should you meet with an accident, you risk overturning and killing someone.

Flattering words and a pleasing countenance: Those who act in this manner are mostly insidious. If they are not harmful to me, then they have a request of me.

The entertainment of singing girls and dancing girls: The gambling of drinking and shouting: All are sharp instruments for ruining one's body and wasting one's family fortune.

Autumn News from Beiping

Cautious

Well-known cross-dressing opera performer Cheng Yushuang, famous in Beijing and Shanghai, has returned north with great acclaim. She has accepted an engagement with the Zhonghe Theater and performs three days a week (Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday). There is not an empty seat. Recently, she has abstained from tobacco and alcohol, and her voice is excellent. Therefore, she is very popular with opera fans. On the evening of December 29th, the business community presented 武家坡 [Wu Jia Po] and 弓硯緣 [The Romance of Bow and Inkstone]. The theater was packed. People were surprised that it was a rare sight. On the 30th, there was a heavy snowstorm. She performed 寶蓮燈 [Baolian Lantern]. The audience numbered over 900 people. On the evening of the 31st, the snowstorm continued. She performed 硃痕記 [Zhu Hen Ji]. The audience numbered over 1,000 people. That evening, Shang Xiaoyun performed the entire 白蛇傳 [Legend of the White Snake] and added 蠟廟 [Wax Temple]. The audience numbered over 300 people. Xun Huisheng performed 元宵謎 [Lantern Festival Riddles]. The audience numbered over 400 people. On New Year's Eve in Beiping, the famous opera performers competed to perform excellent plays. The audience did not let the wind and snow deter them. It was quite a scene of peace and prosperity.

On New Year's Day, Yushuang took an early train to Lü to fulfill her engagement with the Mingxing Theater. She performed 玉堂春 [Yutangchun] on the first evening, 碧玉簪 [Biyu Zan] on the second evening, 柳迎春 [Liu Yingchun] on the third evening, and 金鎖記 [Jin Suo Ji] on the fourth evening. The ticket price was three yuan. All tickets were sold out before the 30th. In addition to studying Sinology, Yushuang is creating new plays. She plans to stage ten plays within a year, all based on having thought and meaning as the criteria. The one that has been completed is 荒山淚 [Tears on a Barren Mountain]. Mr. Li Shizeng praised it greatly and renamed it 祈禱和平 [Pray for Peace]. The ones that are being drafted are named 和平之神 [Goddess of Peace] and 春閨夢 [Spring Boudoir Dreams]. Yushuang's efforts in art are evident. Mr. Li Shizeng once said that a certain director of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, when he saw Yushuang's play in Beiping, said that if Yushuang came to Nanjing to perform, the national affairs could be peaceful. When Yushuang went to Beijing in November to perform charity shows, it coincided with the opening of the Fourth Plenary Session of the North-South Unification. A certain gentleman's prediction came true. Therefore, Beijing called Yushuang the Goddess of Peace.

New Year's New Banquet

Xin Chao

On the evening of the fourth day of the new year, Wang Yansong, the owner of the Da Xin Silk and Satin Bureau, hosted a grand banquet for various circles at the Atlantic, with over 500 people. People from the party, government, businesses, and various other circles were all present. It can truly be called the grandest New Year celebration banquet in Shanghai.

During the banquet, Mr. Wang Yansong explained his ambition in establishing Da Xin, which is to promote domestic goods. Therefore, he spared no effort in collecting all kinds of high-quality American-made silk and satin. Mr. Wang also elaborated on the word "beauty," saying that beauty contains the element of the times. The most fashionable three-inch golden lotuses of the past do not look beautiful now. But beautiful things are abstract. What can represent beauty in the West? As the saying goes, "Buddhas need gold clothes, and people need clothing." It can be seen that clothing can fundamentally represent beauty.

Sitting next to Mr. Wang was a female guest dressed in student attire. Many people mistakenly took her for the hostess. Some even asked Mr. Wang about this. After Mr. Wang explained, it turned out that she was Tang Naixin, the younger sister of Tang Boqi, the director of the Municipal Finance Bureau, and a female reporter for the New Voice News Agency.

Miss Xi, a senior student at a Chinese and Western girls' school, is a Da Xin fashion enthusiast. She orders two or three new outfits from the Da Xin fashion department every month. This has attracted the attention of her classmates. A large number of people have ordered new outfits through her introduction. She also came in person on this day. She said to everyone she met, "New fashions are good." Later, she left before the end of the banquet because she had other business to attend to.

Paris Tales (II)

Liu Ceng, residing in Paris

This film is called "Alibi" (this word is difficult to translate. The general meaning is a defense by a criminal who claims that when the defendant's event occurred, he was in a place outside the crime scene). It was produced in the United States in 1929. We can think that this is probably the last silent film made by Hollywood without the help of a Microphone. This film is quite worthy of attention. I personally regret that there will not be many opportunities to encounter this kind of film in the future.

"Alibi" is by no means an important work. There is no amazing star in it. But this film can be said to be the crystallization of the experience that Americans have gained in the film industry for many years. All places that restrict the actions of actors, and all places that make people feel unreasonable, have been strictly avoided. This film only leaves the spectacle of a tragedy in which mankind is forever fighting and slashing each other. This tragedy is simply shrunk and printed in the struggle between the police and the bandits. The famous film "Night of Chicago" is the representative model of this type of film.

In this film, we can see the pure and simple beauty that those best films possess. The faces of the actors appear very natural on the screen. In fact, I feel that in any film, the plot and interweaving are only of secondary importance. The most important thing is the expression of the actors. Every glance and every raise of the hand are related to the value of the entire film. The actor has to make the audience not feel that they are watching a movie when they watch a movie. They simply live in the movie. They directly participate in the movie. That is a good scene. That is an actor worthy of praise.

The plot of "Alibi" is as follows:

When the screen first opens, a young man is released from prison. Three people are waiting for him at the gate: an elderly man, a prostitute, and a young girl. This elderly man is a hotel owner. To celebrate the young man's release from prison, he has prepared dinner at his home. Everyone drinks happily. Halfway through the drink, a man at the table runs over and asks for the address of the young girl, Joan. Joan generously gave it to him.

When she got home, Joan saw her father (a high-ranking police officer) talking to his friend Inspector Tom. This was the tenth time Tom had asked Joan to marry him. But this was also the tenth time Joan answered him, "I am a policeman's daughter. That is enough. I don't want to be a policeman's wife." Tom left unhappily.

Among the guests that day were old men in their fifties and sixties, as well as young people in their twenties and thirties. Among the guests was a certain writer. He composed a sixteen-character couplet, saying, "There are both men and women. There is no deceit for the old and the young. The eyes and ears are refreshed. Everyone is happy." The four sentences embed the two characters 大新 [Da Xin] and describe the various roles of the guests present at that time, which is very accurate.

Art World News: KMT Second Central Committee members Jing Hengyi and Chen Shuren have always entertained themselves with poetry and books. Even in the midst of tense situations, they indulged in their interests and made many social works. Recently, they have been living together in Tianjin. The number of requests has increased. Therefore, they have jointly ordered a painting agreement to show their intention to reduce their workload. I have now found their agreement and copied it below. The Joint Agreement of Jing Yi Yuan and Chen Shuren: Art is not a perfunctory social matter. There are too many requests. It is unavoidable to be hasty and forgetful. This is for self-encouragement. I also wish to form a painting and calligraphy relationship with general enthusiasts. Starting from the 20th year, the provisional fees are as follows: 1. Jing and Chen jointly painted Xieyi flowers, 10 yuan per square foot. 2. Chen alone does flower-and-bird landscapes, double the price. 3. Jing alone does calligraphy and painting, half price across the board. Couplets are 10 yuan, and other prices are negotiable. Fan faces and albums are calculated as one square foot. Take the item after one month for distant places. (Law News)

Art World News 2: Mr. Chen Gangshu Yunpei, deputy director of the Romantic Society and a famous calligrapher and painter, also known as Tiangang Waiter, studies Shangu and captures his spirit. He is proficient in the Six Canons and is skilled in everything. He is especially good at flower-and-bird paintings, drawing inspiration from Qing Teng, Yunyang, Tiannan, Bei'an, and Xinluo. He has a unique spirit, beautiful without being weak, and charming yet elegant. Therefore, he has long been respected by the art world at home and abroad. In recent years, due to his old age and decline, he often wants to let his hair down and enter the mountains, severing himself from the mundane world, to realize Xiang Ping's unfinished wishes. He reluctantly remains in Shanghai. But his ambition to burn his pen and inkstone has never waned slightly. After a little preparation, he will retire to Zhenjiang, refusing to write or paint again. Therefore, Huang Binhong, Zhang Shanzi, Xiong Songquan, Ma Qizhou, Cai Yimin, Zhang Daqian, and other members of the Romantic Society specially invited him to display dozens of his accumulated masterpieces and fine works at the Xixinglongfang Benyu on Changbang Road and Chongqing Road from the 11th for a limited period. They can also be sold at a low price. Those who like Mr. Zuo and have not yet obtained it should not miss the opportunity. (Yu Jianhua)

Heartwarming Memories (3)(4)(8)

Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen: Earnest Inquiry about Calligraphy, Cui Xiu Visits the Teacher; Generous Talk of Warfare, a Feast in the Brothel for a Female Hero

At that time, the "局" (gathering with singing girls) that was called for came in a continuous stream. Beautiful women surrounded the table, as if holding a round table conference. Zuo Shichen suddenly remembered something. He leaned close to the person sitting next to him, who happened to be Sun Qilei. Zuo Shichen then asked Sun Qilei, "Do you know if this Ms. Ren Peizhen also enjoys calling for "堂唱" (singing performance at a gathering)?" "Look at her, although she is a woman, she likes to be with men. Perhaps she also wants to call for a "局". We might as well ask her." Sun Qilei said, "You reminded me, I almost forgot. Someone just introduced a "堂唱" to her. She didn't refuse, but by the time I left, the "堂唱" hadn't arrived yet. I don't know if she came later." Zuo Shichen said, "Then there's a precedent to follow. Since she called for one, we can also write a "局票丁" (invitation slip) for her. May I ask who introduced her?" Sun Qilei said, "It's the famous courtesan Old Lin Daiyu, who has been well-known in Shanghai for thirty years." Zuo Shichen said, "Really? Then we must call for her. One is a great hero of the Republic of China, and the other is a famous courtesan in Shanghai. Both are famous people. Gathering together, my presence at this banquet today is not in vain." Then he took a "局票" (invitation slip) and a pen and handed them to Sun Qilei, saying, "I'm troubling you. You know she called for Old Lin Daiyu, so it will be easy to get her agreement. If she agrees, you can write it down. It's our first time meeting, so I'm a bit presumptuous." Sun Qilei said, "Speaking of first meeting, isn't it the same for me? However, she is very open and generous. Let me take on this task." Sun Qilei took the pen in hand and said to Ren Peizhen, "On the orders of the host, please invite Mr. Ren to call for a "堂唱". I don't know if the "潚湘妃子" (another name for Lin Daiyu) has come yet." Ren Peizhen said, "No need to call, right? She didn't come just now. I guess she doesn't want to come." Sun Qilei said, "There's no reason why she wouldn't want to come. She comes when anyone calls her. Probably she's just a little late. Do you know how many puffs of opium Old Lin Daiyu smokes? She has to wait until it's dark before she gets up. After she gets up, she has to satisfy her addiction first, and then she can ask about other things. People who smoke opium don't know the time. As long as there's a lamp in front of them, they don't care about anything, no matter how important. It takes two hours for her to satisfy her opium addiction, and then another one or two hours for her to comb her hair and put on makeup. Moreover, she's already reached an age where she has to put in more effort on her makeup. She can't be like those young women who are confident in their youth and just put on light makeup and comb their hair casually. So she always doesn't go out until nine or ten o'clock in the evening. We called her too early just now, so she couldn't come. This time is just the right time. Moreover, she already received a "局票" (invitation slip) earlier, so she will definitely come." Ren Peizhen said, "Then let's try again. I've long heard of her fame. She's a character in Chinese history. It would be good to talk to her."

Gold Price Plummets

Rumors Abound

Atmosphere Turbid

Market Conditions Extremely Perilous Yesterday, January 12th, the gold market situation was extremely chaotic, fluctuating wildly and changing rapidly. The overall market difference was almost 200,000 taels, and the turmoil was extreme. In the end, it plummeted by 20 taels, causing extreme panic and disorientation among the people. Both official and unofficial exchange rates weakened, with the rate of rise slowing down. Banks experienced fewer outflows and more inflows. Trading was varied across the market. Yuan Maoyong, Zhifeng Yong, Yuan Yuan Cheng, and Fu Chang, among others, were net buyers, while Yi Feng Yong, Tai Kangrun, Zhen Changxiang, etc., were largely sellers. Overseas silver markets indicated rising trends in telegraphic reports the day before. Therefore, the gold market initially fell, but then buyers became active, gradually pushing prices upward, briefly exceeding 724 taels. However, due to unfavorable exchange rates and rumors of proposals to rescue plummeting silver prices abroad, the market turned weak and plummeted by 10 taels. The situation was chaotic and unpredictable. The market felt even more complicated, with sudden and violent fluctuations of several taels at a time. The atmosphere was turbulent due to the proliferation of rumors, with the on-again, off-again US loan negotiations causing widespread uncertainty. Subsequently, prices suddenly broke through 710 taels, and trading on the floor became erratic.

Rumors Fueled Disorder It was widely reported that the price of silver for February opening at 715.5 taels in the morning, fell 11.5 taels. (Gross margin fell from 20 to 14-15 taels, then rebounded to 18 taels, but was disorganized and erratic, (and trading was also varied.)) The large bills were all up 16/11, the silver price rose 7/8, private cables added 875. Later, Fu Chang, Yuan Heng, etc., followed up, so the price gradually rose by 5-6 taels, but there were often fluctuations of 2-3 taels. Exchange transactions were mainly sold by peers. Mitsui bought 136,875 worth of March British gold, and Hua Bi bought 137,500 worth of April, then priced it against silver at 75. At 9:20, the price of gold rose to 21.5 taels, and soon fell back 3.5 taels. When the initial quotation was announced, it was increased to 20 taels, which was actually due to the frequent entry and exit of various firms. The listed price of British gold was up 375, Citibank was up 75, Japanese gold was down a small fraction of 4, but the price of gold was still flat, only a little over one tael lower. Afterwards, Yuan Cheng, Fu Yu, Da Lian Bang, etc., bought in, and the internal price of British gold was still stable, so at 10:00 it rose to 724.8 taels. Banks priced 136,25 of February British gold, Mitsui absorbed 1.56 taels of spot from Dalian. Afterwards, the market suddenly turned weak, as Yi Feng Yong, Da De Cheng, and other firms came to sell. In half an hour, the price plummeted by 10 taels. At 10:40, it was 15 taels. Afterwards, the situation was chaotic, with gains and losses of 4-5 taels, amidst the storm, and it was unclear what was happening. At 11:15, it was 23 and rain, with HSBC absorbing 136,875 worth of March British gold, and Shanghai firms selling 625. Subsequently, there was still a 5-tael margin. After 11:30, Yuan Cheng suddenly sold, and the price fell to 17.5 taels. By the close of the market, it was 19.5 taels, and then fell slightly to just over 18 taels, as firms sold off. The quoted price was 760 taels and 0.02, with Japanese gold listed slightly lower by 4%. The amount was reduced from 40 taels to 25-26 taels, then reduced by a small amount of 45 taels, and at noon 41 taels.

The Aftermath of Rumor Mongering After the market opened, it was at 18.5 taels, with gross margins reaching around 20 taels. Due to large forward Indian exchange rates, it fell to 16.5 taels. HSBC and Zhengjin consumed 136,875 worth of March British gold, and Yuan Maoyong and others bought in, rising to 20 taels at 2:10. Then, rumors circulated that the Sino-US loan might be initiated somehow. Because British gold rebounded strongly, banks sold 138,125 worth of April, and the price of gold fell slightly by 2-3 taels. Then, Mitsui suddenly sold 8125 of February, and the selling trend on the floor was particularly strong. Wanxing, Shunli, and Da De Cheng all sold off, so the market fell sharply, reaching 708.5 taels at 3:20. Because Shanghai absorbed 875 of April British gold, Dehua and Mitsui mutually traded 875 of June, and Sumitomo absorbed 8125 of March, it suddenly jumped up by more than 4 taels, reaching 13 taels around 4:00. Firms seeking to cover their positions bought in. After 4:00, it remained in a weak state. Yuan Maoyong, Fu Chang, etc., sold off, and British gold weakened further. March could be settled at 8125, causing a drop of 7-8 taels. At 4:15, it was 705.5 taels, then rose by 2.5 taels. By the market close at 4:30, it was 706.8 taels, a further drop of 20.2 taels compared to the previous Saturday. In subsequent after-hours trading, Fu Chang, Yongheng, Yuan Maoyong, etc., continued to sell, causing a sharp fall to 703 taels, and then 705 taels. The market was unstable and unspeakable, like duckweed drifting with the wind.

Fluctuations of 15 Taels The maximum price for the day was 724.8 taels, and the minimum price was 705.5 taels (according to listed prices), a difference of 19.3 taels. The quoted price was reduced from 40 taels to 53-54 taels. Before and after the close, the market was settled twice. Discount Market: Tight and Slack Phenomena

At the end of the year, the financial sector usually adopts a policy of contraction. Because account settlements and loan repayments were held in two phases last year, all year-end payments have not yet been settled. Therefore, the current situation remains the same as in previous years. Transactions between silver and money businesses continue to flow in and out, and must be settled after the Lunar New Year. This leads to a mixed situation of tightness and slack in the market. Western discounts seem to be falling again, while silver credit is very strong. Overdrafts feel quite tight. However, the market is not chaotic and there are no other unexpected changes.

Food: River Downstream Rice Market - Southern Stability and Northern Firmness

Zhabei Yesterday, a few boats of inland rice arrived, but were still sparse. Sales from all directions were extremely active. There was little white glutinous rice of high quality, and the top price rose by 0.1 yuan, opening at 13.7 yuan. The special glutinous rice disk face was hovering around 14 yuan, with no major changes. The purchasing sentiment for thin rice was acceptable, and the price was close to rising by 0.1 yuan. There were few shipments and storage of mutton glutinous rice, and sales were average. Although the Du Township sharp cargo was declining, the sales market was not smooth. The general trend was that only high-quality goods rose by half a foot. There was no particularly high-quality rice from Bian Yuan. Ordinary high-quality rice from Gao Yuan was traded quite a bit, and the market price was rising beyond 0.1 yuan. Yin Yuan was stable and uneventful. High-quality goods opened at 12 yuan.

Shanghai South Yesterday, over ten boats arrived, and the market sentiment was weak. Regular glutinous rice was extremely scarce, and the top market price barely opened at 13 yuan or so. Ordinary machine glutinous rice such as Su Tong etc., were all fixed. The average and lower-quality ones need to be reduced by about 0.1 yuan, a bleak situation. South Gang green angle and other thin rice and early rice, had little arrival and sale, their prices remained flat, while central passes received small discounts, which was related to the sunny weather. The street retail of Mutton Du Sharp was acceptable, with slow arrivals, and stable trends. Besides the steady high-quality rice from Bian Chu Yuan, the remaining rice had a mediocre momentum.

Guest Hsien Rice Continues to Improve

Inland river sources decrease, street sales become the main outlet

Prices of Ji Wan rice and other varieties rise by a few cents

Yesterday, the market situation for guest hsien rice was particularly favorable, showing an upward trend. This was due to the freezing of inland river channels, which reduced the supply of Du rice to the city. Moreover, the number of arriving boats had decreased recently, leading to a shift towards purchasing guest hsien rice. Yesterday, over two thousand packages of Jiangxi Ji Wan rice and two hundred packages of Ji Zao rice were selected and purchased. Buyers from Ningbo were also gradually becoming active. Four to five hundred packages of Hunan red rice and other varieties were also purchased on the market yesterday. The arrival of guest yuan rice was limited, and with the decrease in Du yuan rice supply, the market also showed an upward trend. Yesterday, buyers from Xiamen purchased around three hundred packages of Xiang-Gan Ji Yuan rice. The listed prices were: Jiangxi Ji Wan rice, eleven yuan and six cents to ten yuan and eight cents; Ji Zao rice, ten yuan and four cents; Ji Yuan rice, thirteen yuan; Hunan Ji Hong rice, ten yuan and two cents and six fen; Red rice, nine yuan and seven cents; Ji Yuan rice, twelve yuan; Nanjing Ji Yuan rice, ten yuan and five fen. All prices were a few cents higher than the previous market prices.

Wheat Prices Plummet

Yesterday, after the opening of the futures wheat market in the morning and afternoon, all months experienced a sharp decline. The price of gold had fallen by nearly twenty to thirty taels from its peak, leading to a significant increase in exchange rates. Therefore, for the distant months, the short sellers, based on contracted wheat purchases, could still approach the actual price. For example, the combined price of Australian wheat was only about four qian, so selling pressure resumed smoothly, while the long positions retreated. The market was largely bearish. Looking at the future rise and fall, it will depend on the situation abroad. As a result, this month's price fell by six fen compared to the previous weekend, February fell by one qian, March fell by nine fen, April fell by one qian, May fell by seven fen, and the price of new wheat in June remained unchanged.

Reasons for the Sharp Decline in the Flour Market

Surplus of foreign wheat...Gold price reversal...Short positions increased

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, all months experienced another sharp decline. Due to the surplus of wheat in England and the United States, they were entering a state of close competition, leading to negotiations for large loans to China. According to the rumored news, it is unlikely to become a reality. However, the surplus of wheat in the domestic market is an undeniable fact. Therefore, people's confidence suddenly weakened, and selling pressure increased. Furthermore, with the reversal of gold prices and a slight increase in interest rates, short sellers inevitably became more enthusiastic. Therefore, the overall market situation, shrouded in this atmosphere, once again moved towards a sharp decline. As a result, this month's price fell by three fen and two and a half li compared to the previous weekend, February fell by three fen and two and a half li, March and April fell by four fen, May fell by four fen and two and a half li, and June fell by three fen and seven and a half li.

Sugar Market: Japanese Sugar Sales Flourish with 40,000 Bags

Market prices slightly stabilized as a result...New green sugar rose by eight taels and two qian

Yesterday, there were no telegrams from the sugar market production areas regarding Cuban spot sugar and New York sugar futures. Java spot and futures prices remained unchanged. In the guild market, the buying interest for Dutch sugar No. 24 coarse grain white was still strong. The initial asking price was higher, but as trading continued, the transaction price remained at one tael and six qian and a half. Cuban foreign sugar was nine taels and one qian, Dutch red sugar No. 8 was nine taels and one qian and a half. The market was still firm. Japanese sugar YT mark was ten taels and seven qian, Minghua goods were ten taels and seven qian to six qian and a half, YP mark was eleven taels, YRO mark was ten taels and two qian, Meiji goods were ten taels and two qian and a half, YP mark was eleven taels and one qian, J mark was eleven taels and two qian and a half. The market was relatively stable. The factory price for Dali sugar was four yuan and seven jiao, although a telegram had been sent, confirmation was still pending. Meiji goods for March delivery opened at 12,000 bags, priced at 4.6 yuan in Japanese gold plus tax. Minghua sugar for February delivery was 10,000 bags, priced at 6.7 yuan in Japanese gold including tax, which was very popular. Although Panjin Faji opened sales of 2,000 bags of coarse grain white spot goods, priced at 10 taels and six qian and a half. Deda Hao sold 48 bags of Xiamen ice flower green sugar, priced at 9 taels and 7 qian.
