Northern and Southern Goods: Dried Longan and Golden Needles Continue to Rise in Price

(Dried Longan) Due to recent lack of arrivals, sales have become more active, and the interest of various firms has intensified, so the market price has repeatedly increased. The previous evening, trading continued to rise again, with ordinary goods rising from 29 taels to 31 taels. Slightly inferior goods only fluctuated by a few qian. Gaozhuang opened at 47 taels. The future market has a tendency to tighten further. (Golden Needles) Currently, winter sales are brisk, and demand from Guangdong and Hong Kong is quite good. The previous batch of goods has been sold out, and various firms are adding supplies from Shanghai. The trading is exceptionally tight. Yesterday, another batch opened, priced at 25 taels and a half to 23 taels, exceeding the market price. Therefore, the selling price has also increased accordingly.

Processors Decide to Increase the Price of Dried Longan

Due to the recent decrease in arrivals of selected dried longan and the rumor of increased land prices and taxes, and the difficulty in making profits in the Shanghai market, the trade association convened a meeting of various firms yesterday to decide on a slight increase in prices to avoid losses. The market prices for each grade are listed below: Top grade 30 taels, Heavenly grade 22 taels, Tianhong 16 taels, Sales grade 12 taels, Regular grade 20 taels, Top baldy 32 taels, Baldy one 22 taels, Baldy baldy 17 taels, Bubble yuan 10 taels.

Shanghai White Silk Steadil Rises in Price

B Grade Highest Price Reaches One Thousand and Thirty Taels

Yesterday, the Shanghai white silk market continued to rise gradually. European, American, and Japanese firms were actively purchasing and bidding up prices. The price was highest for goods purchased by Mitsui, reaching 1030 taels. This market trend may be influenced by the sharp rise in gold prices.

Jinlong, Jardine, and China Tea Company purchased 350 boxes of Qimen and Wenzhou black teas. The market price has fallen by three or four taels compared to before. The tea market trend is still downward.

Coal: Sales of Fushun Coal from Three Mines are Strong

The sales of Fushun coal, among the three types of anthracite coal, have been strong since the New Year. Buyers from inland areas, such as the Hangzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou region, are purchasing the most. The purchasing power of small factories in Shanghai is also strong. The average daily transaction volume is about two hundred tons. However, the coal inventory of each warehouse is only about two thousand tons. At a time when gold prices are soaring and the Japanese exchange rate is increasing, the selling price has risen by more than two taels. The opening price in the market yesterday rose from twelve taels and a half to thirteen taels and seven qian and a half per ton.

The Shanghai Caoye Society at 34 Feilun Road and its branch at 21 Damalu Lane, Chenghuang Temple, Hangzhou, will simultaneously hold a recruitment of members from the 10th of this month to February 12th. Business News

The Caoye Society at 34 Feilun Road announced that the original manuscript paper and other items published by the society will be discounted for five days starting from the 15th of this month. Those who subscribe to the newspaper within five days will pay nine jiao for the whole year, including postage, for local subscribers and one yuan and one jiao for out-of-town subscribers. They will also receive a copy of Tang Zenghao's "Solo Singing". Other books will be discounted from 30% to 50%. Original manuscript paper will be sold at a reduced price of two jiao per hundred sheets. Bound volumes of "Caoye" volumes 2 and 3 will be sold at a reduced price of three jiao.

The Lincoln Motor Company announced that it uses various special tests in its factory to ensure that the leather and decorative fabrics used in the car meet the fixed highest standards of Lincoln car manufacturing. The testing method uses light similar to sunlight and cold than ice, and a stronger tensile force than a famous breed to measure it. After testing, if it is found to be qualified, it will be used to manufacture Lincoln cars. The leather used in the car must be able to withstand climates colder than zero degrees without cracking. This type of leather can also have good performance in the northwestern states, where the weather is extremely cold. It must also undergo a strength test to determine its solid quality and durability. Various fabrics used to decorate the car are illuminated with intense purple light, so there is no risk of discoloration even in places with strong tropical sunlight. The texture must be uniform, and it is torn open with a powerful machine to explore whether it can withstand wear and tear. The springs used in the car body seat must also undergo the same rigorous testing as above to increase the comfort of riding. A machine with a 50-pound force bullet strikes 25,000 to 30,000 times to test its elasticity, whether it is sufficient to make the car durable and comfortable in the future.

The Overseas Chinese Bathhouse at the new North Gate of MinGuo Road announced that this bathhouse was solely funded and established by Mr. Wu Guilin. The layout is elegant, the reception is thoughtful, and the potted plants and fresh flowers are beautifully decorated. In addition, the seats and bathrooms are clean, spacious, and the prices are low. Therefore, the bathers are unusually crowded, and there is quite a busy scene.

The Sanyou Industrial Society announced that its Hangzhou Gongchenqiao Sanyou Factory will be closed for the Gengxin New Year and will switch to following the Gregorian calendar. It also invited people from all walks of life to a New Year's banquet on the 6th to promote it. Attendees included the newly appointed Mayor Chen Qihuai, Section Chief Wu of the Social Affairs Bureau, Director Liu of the Provincial Water Police Bureau, Director Zhu of the Public Security Bureau's Third District, Chen Guohua of the Federation of National Goods Factories, and financial figures such as Zhang Xuren of Chufeng Bank, Jin Bohou of the Salt Industry Bank, and Shi Qiansun of the Continental Bank. Others, such as Fang Zonghan of Gaoyitai and Cheng Weicheng of Cheng Songmao, and Yu Tianshun of Dafeng, also attended together, totaling about seventy or eighty people. General Manager Shen Jiucheng, Deputy General Manager Chen Wanyun, and Hangzhou Factory Director Qian Xizhen warmly received them and led them to visit the newly completed new spinning factory, weaving factory, finishing and dyeing factory, and the original spinning factory. The scale is grand and the layout is neat. The general manager reported that the original spinning factory, due to its old construction and insufficient lighting, often felt major shortcomings in its work. After accurate costing last year, the newest and most rational chemical spinning and weaving factories were built, adding new spinning machines and thousands of looms and complete dyeing and finishing machines, in order to improve the quality of goods and reduce consumption. Various constructions over the past year have only now reached the production period. Coinciding with the government's implementation of tariff cuts, domestic national goods factories have obtained a glimmer of light, so they will go further and convert the original yarn factory into a wool spinning and weaving department, manufacturing various wool fabrics to contribute to the nation, in order to recover some of the losses. The factory spent about 600,000 or more on various construction projects and the addition of machines last year, making it truly the only complete factory in Zhejiang Province.

The Far East Cleaning Institute Export Department at 93 Sichuan Road and 24 Central Road House announced that since its manager, Bai Jinhuai, introduced the hand warmer, sales have been extremely brisk. Wholesale and retail buyers have come to purchase them in droves. Even if there is vibration, it will not be damaged. It is not only warm for a long time, but it also uses very little liquid medicine, and the price is low. Each one is sold for only three yuan and five jiao, plus a black or purple velvet bag. Each large bottle of liquid medicine is sold for thirty-five cents. Each lamp head for the heater is sold separately for fifty cents. Calligraphy and Painting News

The Tiangang Waiter Personal Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition announced that Mr. Tiangang Chen Gangshu's calligraphy and painting are exquisite and have long been respected by the art world at home and abroad. His calligraphy studies Huang Tingjian and obtains his spirit. His paintings are skilled in landscapes, figures, and animals, especially in flowers and birds, with lively postures and elegant brushstrokes. He draws from Bai Yang, Qing Teng, and Xinluo, but does not imitate the ancients. Therefore, those who seek his works come one after another. Recently, due to old age and declining strength, Mr. Chen intends to burn his pens and inkstones and retire to Zhenjiang. Huang Binhong, Zhang Shanzi, Xiong Songquan, Ma Qizhou, Cai Yimin, Yu Jianhua, Zhang Daqian, and other families from the Lanman Society specially requested him to exhibit dozens of his usual outstanding masterpieces at the Xixinglong Workshop at the intersection of Changbang Road and Chongqing Road for a week, starting from the 11th, and they will be available at a cheap price.
